Central Government and National Government Memorial Week 73

Central Party Headquarters: On the 31st at 9:00 AM, the Central Party Headquarters held the 53rd weekly memorial service for the late Premier Sun Yat-sen in the grand auditorium. Approximately 500 to 600 people attended, including central committee members, department and bureau staff, and guests. Chairman Hu Hanmin, after the ritual bowing, gave a report, stating that the reactionary warlords' betrayal of the Party and the nation was now undeniably exposed. What was strange was that Chen Gongbo and others were busily traveling between Peiping and Taiyuan, engaging in unconscious alliances with Yan Xishan. Yan Xishan, having entrenched himself in the north for over a decade, was accustomed to the warlord tricks of past years. His mind was filled only with feudal thoughts and he did not recognize the Party's principles or revolutionary spirit. Therefore, no matter how he pretended, he would inevitably take a path of counter-revolution or non-revolution. As for Chen Gongbo and others, they had always been skilled in opportunism, sometimes being Kuomintang members, sometimes collaborating with Chen Jiongming, sometimes aligning with the Communist Party, and now, using the excuse of seeking a way out, they were cooperating with the most cunning of the warlords. At best, they were only exploiting each other to seek temporary gains. Politically, they would not have a long lifespan. The result would only be the abandonment of their character and the hastening of their downfall. Their biggest mistakes were: (1) deviating from the Party's principles and the late Premier's teachings. They completely failed to understand the late Premier's instructions on saving the country through the Party, governing the country through the Party, and building the country through the Party, as well as the revolutionary process that must go through the military and tutelage stages. They only sought a way to advance their careers, not hesitating to become traitors to the Party. (2) greatly despising the people, believing that with power in hand, they could arbitrarily oppress the masses and do whatever they pleased, with an attitude of "let others curse, I will be a good official myself." They did not know that there was true right and wrong in the universe, and true likes and dislikes in public opinion. How prominent was the Preparatory Society during Yuan Shikai's imperial ambitions, and how verbose were Wu Jinglian's arguments when Cao Kun bribed votes? But what was the result? It can be seen that anyone who violates justice and goes against the will of the people is bound to fail. At this time, Yan Xishan is using three or five people despised by the Kuomintang, as well as Duan Qirui, Feng Yuxiang, Wu Peifu, and others as puppets, hoping to become a temporary dictator himself. But Yan's abilities are far inferior to Duan, Feng, and Wu. Duan still knew that the country needed a strong government and was willing to bear considerable responsibility. Although Feng was hated by the people in the north, he was also feared by the people. Wu was brave in battle and did not want to use others. Yan, on the other hand, has not only betrayed the government but also wants to use cunning tricks to use others as his tools. This kind of behavior is not worth mentioning. Although the central government wants to reform such people, it is impossible. It can only fundamentally strengthen the Party's power, be determined to eliminate the warlords, and consolidate the foundation of the Party and the country. After the report, the meeting adjourned at 10:30 AM.

National Government: On the same day at 10:00 AM, the National Government held a weekly memorial service for the late Premier Sun Yat-sen. Tan Yankai, Gu Yingfen, Yi Peiji, Zhang Wohua, Liu Ruiheng, Zheng Hongnian, Zhang Nanxian, He Yingqin, Zhu Peide, He Yaozu, Chen Yi, Zhou Yawei, Zhang Yuanhu, Liu Jiwen, and all staff of the National Government's civilian officials, military attachés, and adjutant offices, totaling over 200 people, attended. Chairman Tan Yankai, after the ritual bowing, had Secretary Qian Changzhao give the following political report: "[The reconstruction of Tokyo, Japan, has been completed. This reminds me of the spring of 1924 when I traveled to Japan. At that time, Tokyo had just experienced an earthquake. The roads and businesses were uneven, and the houses, except for large buildings such as the Imperial Palace and the Imperial Hotel, were mostly collapsed in the east and fallen in the west. The Japanese people suffered great sacrifices in that natural disaster, but they showed no signs of decline. Their spirit of perseverance and determination is truly admirable. I once said that their recovery period was not far away. Now, the reconstruction of Tokyo has been completed after six and a half years and costing 800 million yuan. The Japanese government and the people have a unified spirit, burying their heads in construction, silently completing unprecedented work. During this period, they encountered many difficulties, but they still proceeded according to the original plan because they were very confident. The original plan was very detailed and had already taken into account manpower and financial resources, and manpower and financial resources could be concentrated on the original plan. Today, the completion of the construction is such an honor. Japan is like this, and our country should work hard. Recently, the world's material construction, those with sufficient manpower and financial resources, and using large knives and axes to construct, are the United States. Those with considerable manpower and financial resources, and extremely cautious and orderly, are the United Kingdom. Those without sufficient manpower and financial resources, but using a spirit of perseverance and determination to construct, are Japan and Germany. The construction of the United States has

Page 10

sometimes bordered on wastefulness, the construction of the United Kingdom has been too cautious, and the construction of Japan and Germany is the most worthy of emulation. This time, Japan's reconstruction of its capital is a good example. Although Germany was restricted everywhere after the war, it returned to its pre-war state in less than ten years, which is also unattainable. Our country's manpower and financial resources are still far inferior to those of Japan and Germany. Only by emulating their spirit of perseverance and determination can we hope for the future of construction. The importance of Hulunbuir is not well known to the general public. The area is vast and sparsely populated, and industries such as agriculture, mining, forestry, and animal husbandry have not yet been developed. As long as we find ways to improve them, economic progress will surely be rapid. Previously, the central government and Hulunbuir were very estranged, and imperialists took the opportunity to entice and instigate. Recently, the central government has paid special attention, and Hulunbuir has also sent representatives to Beijing. In the future, border worries can be reduced. Nepal's dispatch of troops into Tibet has a great impact on our country. The central government has decided on countermeasures, which are not convenient to announce at the moment. In short, the central government is very cautious about this matter, striving to resolve the dispute and consolidate the border. However, I have one feeling, that is, we are too unclear about the border situation. When incidents occur, not only is the truth difficult to discern, but there is also very little reference material. However, imperialists have various preparations, eyeing us covetously. How dangerous this is! This year's Mongolian and Tibetan Conference hopes to finalize the major policies. At the same time, I also hope that people with ambition will launch a movement and go to Mongolia and Tibet in teams. Yan Feng's rebellion, sometimes wanting to take the false post of commander-in-chief, sometimes wanting to organize a false government in Peiping, is driven by greed and acting in a rush, without a definite plan. In short, the more tricks they play in their rebellion, the faster their defeat. Now Yan Feng is facing economic difficulties, lacking pay and ammunition. Although some say that foreign banks are willing to lend them money, this news is not necessarily true, because if it is true, then foreign banks are truly foolish beyond comparison, because this kind of loan will never be repaid in principal and interest, and the only cost is the resentment of our people. As for the central government's response to this rebellion, everything is prepared, but because this is the key to the success of the revolution, the attitude taken is particularly steady. The people should not panic, and various rumors should not be easily believed."

Detailed Account of Chairman Chiang's Visit to Hangzhou from Ningbo 74

To Deliver a Speech at the Provincial Party Headquarters' Memorial Week

National Government Chairman Chiang Kai-shek, accompanied by his wife Madame Soong Mei-ling, Vice Minister of the Navy Chen Shaokuan, and others, took the Chu Tai warship from Nanjing via Shanghai back to his ancestral home in Fenghua on the 21st. It was originally scheduled to come to Hangzhou on the 26th. Zhejiang Provincial Government Chairman Zhang Jingjiang, Civil Affairs Commissioner Zhu Jiahua, Education Commissioner Chen Bulei, Secretary-General Shen Shiyuan, and others all went to Fenghua to welcome him. Later, the provincial government received a telegram from Fenghua, saying that Chairman Chiang would leave Fenghua for Hangzhou on the morning of the 30th. The military and police were immediately ordered to protect the route in sections. The Xixing section was the responsibility of the 1st Regiment of the Infantry Training Corps. The Jianggan section was the responsibility of Brigade Commander Liu, Regiment Commander Lai, Police Chief Li, and others, who personally led the 3rd Regiment of the Security Team, the Cavalry Patrol Team, the Provincial Police Brigade, the 1st District Team of the Water Police, and the police of the Hangzhou County Public Security Bureau, providing thorough protection.

Yesterday (30th) at 1:00 PM, party and government figures from all walks of life in the provincial capital arrived at Jianggan to welcome him. Those who arrived included Provincial Government Chairman Zhang Jingjiang, Madame Zhang, and their sons and daughters, Civil Affairs Commissioner Zhu Jiahua, Education Commissioner Chen Bulei, Provincial Government Secretary-General Shen Shiyuan, Provincial Party Headquarters Executive Committee members Ye Suzhong, Xu Shaodi, Chen Xihui, Zhang Qiang, Yang Yunfang, Qing Ru, Provincial Party Headquarters Supervisory Committee member Hu Jianzhong, Construction Department Secretary Chief Huo Baoshu, Security Office Chief Zhu Siming, Mayor Zhou Xiangxian, Tobacco Tax Bureau Chief Liu Hao, and Lai Gang, Shen Chang, and others, totaling over one hundred people.

Chairman Chiang and his party departed from Xikou by car at 8:00 AM yesterday morning and arrived in Ningbo at 9:20 AM. They briefly rested at the Chiang Supervising Office. At 10:10 AM, they took the prepared decorated cars from Ningbo to Cao'e, where they had lunch in the car. They stopped at the Wufu station for ten minutes to inspect the 4th Regiment of the 1st Brigade of the Central Infantry Training Corps. At 11:30 AM, they arrived at Baiguan and immediately crossed the Cao'e River. At 2:00 PM, they took the No. 105 car provided by the Highway Bureau from Wuyun and arrived at the Xixing riverbank at 3:40 PM. The car drove directly onto the ship at the dock. At that time, Xiaoshan County Magistrate Du and Provincial Highway Bureau Chief Chen Ticheng were also on board waiting. At 3:45 PM, when Chairman Chiang's car arrived directly at the dock ship, it was raining heavily. Chiang and his wife Soong Mei-ling got out of the car and nodded to the welcomers one by one, then immediately boarded the ship. There were two tugboats prepared by the provincial government, one for Chairman Chiang and one for his entourage. At 4:17 PM, the tugboat was towed to the riverbank by the Yi He warship. At that time, the welcomers were all standing by the ship in the rain. First, Provincial Government Secretary-General Shen stepped forward to salute, and the important figures all came forward to pay their respects. Chiang and Madame Soong nodded in return, then immediately took the car prepared by the provincial government, accompanied by Adjutant Wang Shiyu, and drove directly to Chiang Villa. The military and police along the way held their guns in salute. No fewer than sixty or seventy welcoming cars also went to Chiang Villa in West Lake. Those who came with Chairman Chiang, in addition to his wife Madame Soong, included German advisor Fischen, Naval Vice Minister Chen Shaokuan, Secretary Gao Lingbai, Rong Baofeng, Mao Qingxiang, Zhang Jiaoyuzhang Zhizhong, Song Zi'an, and Guard Captain Jiang Fushou. It was reported that after arriving in Hangzhou, he would immediately inspect the 155th Brigade stationed in Hangzhou and the various units of the 1st Brigade of the Central Military Officers' Training Corps, but due to the rain, the inspection was changed to start this morning. According to Naval Acting Minister Chen, Chiang also plans to attend the opening ceremony of the National Games tomorrow (1st), and then return to Nanjing. Today (31st) at 9:00 AM, the Provincial Party Headquarters and the Provincial Government held a joint memorial week in the Party Headquarters auditorium. Chairman Chiang also attended and participated. After the ritual bowing, Chairman Chiang gave the following speech: "Comrades, I have made some contributions to the party and government of this province. I will take this opportunity to speak during today's memorial week. Speaking of the party and government of this province, in any aspect, it is more advanced than other provinces. This is all due to the efforts of everyone, which have resulted in the good results of this model province. I also share in the glory. Regarding party affairs, the work of the Provincial Party Headquarters has been very good. The organization of the county party headquarters and sub-branches is also quite sound. I have not been to Zhejiang for a year. In this year, material construction has been quite remarkable, which is very gratifying. However, these good things are our responsibilities, and there is no need for much praise. Regarding the political aspect, Zhejiang has focused on local autonomy and implemented the village-li system and the baojia law for the past year. This was originally an important task during the period of political tutelage. The land declaration is also an important event in local autonomy and is the first step in land survey. When implementing a new policy for the first time, the public's suspicion is unavoidable. The handling of the land declaration in Zhejiang this time has generally been without problems. However, the registration fee of seven copper coins for one house is unprecedented in Chinese history. The registration fee for one or two fen of land is the same as for one mu of land, which makes the people feel quite painful. There is no difference between people with one or two mu of land and those with ten or one hundred mu of land. The people think it is a bit unfair. The government should pay attention to this and study a way to improve it. Secondly, according to what I know, the lijia heads of the village-li system in Zhejiang do not actually do anything, they are nominally existent. In the future, we should find ways to make them live up to their names and should be helped by the county party headquarters and sub-branches, using passive means to achieve active purposes. We must not use very strong force to interfere with the environment, but must use good intentions to persuade. For the evil forces in the locality, as long as they do not oppress the poor and do not monopolize lawsuits, it is not necessary to eliminate them completely, making them unable to exist. When doing things, one must know when to stop. In addition, regarding the current situation, I can also briefly report a few points. The barriers between revolution and counter-revolution are becoming clearer day by day. In the past, corrupt and deteriorating elements, wearing the mask of revolution, were mixed in with our party. Who is

a comrade and who is an enemy, we could not distinguish clearly. Now that their true colors are gradually being exposed, the future of the revolution is brighter. I often say that the more obvious the reactionary forces are, the faster the revolution will succeed, and the more confident we will be. This is not boasting. I heard that Yan Xishan is scheduled to take the false post of Commander-in-Chief of the Chinese Army tomorrow. Yan's purpose this time is to use all factions to eliminate the Kuomintang. It is a pity that the Reorganization Faction has not yet realized this. We are desperate for the leaders of the Reorganization Faction to be obsessed with confusion, but for the young people of the Reorganization Faction, we should warn them, so that they can still maintain their position and history in the revolution. Now the other side is uniting all reactionary forces to rise up in chaos. The content is very complex. Now the government is still adhering to the principle of peace and using very simple forces to deal with them, so it is very optimistic about the situation, and it is expected that the country will be truly unified by the end of this year and they will definitely be eliminated. The opening of the National Games tomorrow is the first grand event since the Chinese Revolution. It is very meaningful. It not only exercises the national physique, but also promotes the national spirit. Zhejiang held a West Lake Expo last year, and this year it is holding the National Games. If there is a chance to participate tomorrow, I have a proposal, which is to promote domestic goods. During the conference, we should focus on sports and promote domestic goods, which is of great benefit to the future of our country. I hope you will help me complete this grand event."

Han Fuju Leads Troops Through Xuzhou 75

General Headquarters Moves to Jining

The Third Route Army Garrisons Western Shandong

Xuzhou Correspondence: Han Fuju, under orders from the Central Government, is proceeding with the planned transfer of the Third Route Army to Western Shandong. The General Headquarters is being moved to Jining. Mr. Han himself, along with staff from the General Headquarters and some personnel from the Provincial Government, departed eastward by special train on the morning of the 29th. There were slight delays along the way at Lanfeng, Neihuang, and Liuhe. In the evening, the railway reported that Han's train was about to arrive in Xuzhou. Liu Zhi, as well as Xu Tingyao, acting commander of the 1st Division, Chief of Staff Liu Yaoyang, Qian Zongze, director of the Longhai Railway Bureau, Huang Cishan, the county magistrate, Qiao Shizhao, the head of the Public Security Bureau, and Han's wife, all went to the station to welcome him. At 11:10 PM, Han's special train entered the station, accompanied by a loud military band. After the train stopped, Han alighted first and shook hands and exchanged pleasantries with Liu Zhi and the welcoming party. At that time, Han told reporters that he had come east under orders, the General Headquarters had arrived with the train, the troops were still gathering in eastern Henan, and there were no troops from his command west of Bian. He himself planned to stay in Xuzhou for a day, to consult with Commander Liu and to request instructions from the Commander, before determining his next course of action. He also said that some of the Provincial Government personnel remained in the province to maintain order. There was still a small remnant of Sun Dianying's troops in Guide. He had not formally attacked them, in order to avoid harming the people. Han then borrowed Liu Zhi's car and entered the city, and the welcomers dispersed. Han lodged at the Huayuan Hotel that evening. Those who came with Han in the same train included Li Zongbi, Chief of Staff of the General Headquarters, Zhang Shaotang, Secretary, Li Shuchun, Commissioner of the Civil Affairs of the Provincial Government, Wang Xiangrong, Commissioner of the Finance of the Provincial Government, and others. There were about thirty cars in total, fully loaded with guards, vehicles, equipment, and other items. Hai Tao, who had traveled from Nanjing to Bian under Chiang's orders to see Han, had also arrived in Xuzhou before Han. Hai told reporters that he and Commander Han had left Bian for Xuzhou one after the other. Han would be going to Jining within days, and he himself, because Ma Hongkui was in command, had gone to Jinan, and would be going to Jinan from Xuzhou within days to meet with Ma before returning to Nanjing to report back.

On the morning of the 30th, the reporter visited Li Zongbi on the train and asked Mr. Li to talk about the following: the retreat of the headquarters to the east under orders was a planned project. Since the conflict between the headquarters and the Wan Xuancai's troops in Zhongmu, Wan had sent a representative to Bian, but it seemed that his intention was to spy on the situation rather than to explain the misunderstanding. The headquarters had been retreating eastward since the day before yesterday (28th) and had completely left Bian by yesterday (29th). Before leaving Bian, it was learned that a brigade of cavalry from the Northwest Army had arrived at the Wan Xuancai Division at the forefront of Zheng, and it had now reached Bian. The army concentrated in eastern Henan and the Second Route Army in western Xu had joined the defense line. The equipment and troops transported by train in the headquarters consisted of a total of ten trains, all of which arrived in Xuzhou with the Commander's train and were successively transferred to western Shandong. The Commander would also transfer to Jining. The reporter asked about Shi Yousan's recent attitude. Li said that Mr. Shi did not seem to understand the doctrine very well, but he had not made any overt expressions. At that time, the trains that had arrived in Xuzhou with Han had already headed north one after another.

Commander Liu, taking advantage of Han's visit to Xuzhou, arranged a banquet on the evening of the 30th to welcome Han. All the senior generals and provincial commissioners who came with Han were invited. The banquet was very lively. Han's special train was scheduled to depart northward that evening. It was reported that the Third Route Army and the Fifteenth Route Army would form a joint defense in western Shandong. As for the western section of the route, Han said that there was not much damage and there were no major changes in the military situation. After shortening the defense line, the strength would be more concentrated. The rebel army could be wiped out in one fell swoop by tilting its nest. (30th)

Deng Ying's Troops Recapture Fenyi County 76

Provincial Party Headquarters Asks Central Government for Troops to Suppress Bandits

Nanchang correspondence on the 29th: Fenyi is located in western Jiangxi, between Xinyu, Anfu, Yichun, and Wanzai. After Anfu and Wanzai successively sounded the alarm, the county was also in imminent danger. At dawn on March 20, about 1,000 troops under Peng Dehuai, with 700-800 guns and 4 machine guns, entered the county seat. At that time, there was only one company of troops stationed in the city. Due to the disparity in numbers, the city fell to the bandits at 11:00 AM, and the order was in great chaos. All the county government officials disguised themselves and fled to Xinyu and sent a telegram to the province asking for help. After receiving the telegram, the provincial government specially dispatched Deng Ying's independent 16th Brigade from Xiajiang and Xinyu to suppress the bandits. The 2nd and 4th regiments of the brigade arrived in Fenyi on the 22nd. Peng's bandits personally led their troops to resist, and the fighting was fierce. Deng's troops bravely suppressed them and recaptured the county seat the next day. It was heard that Peng's bandits had the potential to flee from Binjiang and harass Yichun. In addition to sending troops to pursue them, Brigade Commander Deng also telegraphed the 1st Regiment in Anfu to open up to Yichun to block them. The provincial party headquarters believes that the province is adjacent to six provinces, and the relationship with the southeast is very important for security. Recently, bandits and communists have been rampant, and they have repeatedly fallen into cities. Countless people have died and been injured. However, the number of troops stationed in the province is limited, and it is difficult to take care of both. Therefore, at the fourth regular meeting on the 28th, it was decided to appoint Liu and Zou as members to go to Beijing to petition the central government to dispatch capable troops to Jiangxi to suppress the bandits. As for the provincial government, it regards bandit suppression as the only way out for the province. Therefore, the expenses of various agencies are planned to be reduced for the purpose of bandit suppression. At the same time, because the establishment of four guard regiments and the construction of shallow-water warships are urgently needed, the Finance Department has issued 1 million yuan of circulating notes to relieve the current emergency.

Xiang Communist Leader Ye Kui Arrested and Executed 77

Changsha correspondence on the 27th: Ye Kui, the leader of the communist riots in Changsha, who gathered thousands of people in Lushanzhen across the river and burned and killed for two years, had a reward of 2,000 yuan put on his head by Zhou Lan, Cheng Qian, Lu Di, and others when they presided over the Xiang government, but he had never been captured because of his numerous party members and good information. Recently, because the communists had been active in the two lakes again, and He Long had invaded Ouchi from western Hubei, looking to attack Changli, Ye Kui was ordered by the party center to be responsible for launching riots in Nanhua, Lianan, and other counties to respond to He Long. Ye then went to the Nanhua area to make arrangements and was then detected by Ding Duo, the commander of the temporary bandit suppression in Lushanzhen, Changsha. The first team leader Zheng Shuchen was immediately dispatched with 20 soldiers, each carrying a pistol, disguised as plainclothes, and rushed to Fuxingyuan in Huarong County that night to find Ye was gathering party members at Daximiao to hold a meeting. Team Leader Zheng reported to the Nanhua County Defense Bureau, which dispatched a team of soldiers to rush to the temple in the rain at 10 p.m. on the 12th and surrounded the temple, but it was too early, and the party members had not yet arrived, so only Ye Kui and Ye's secretary-general Yi Shunding, and party members Ren Man, Wang Mazi, Liu Dai three, and five others were captured. When He Jian was informed, in addition to immediately awarding a reward of 2,000 yuan, he ordered Ye Kui and Yi Shunding to be escorted to the province for interrogation, and they were sent to the province on the 20th and handed over to the Qingxiang Command Headquarters, which interrogated them four times in succession. According to Ye's confession, he was ordered by the Communist Party Central Committee, and he and He Long were responsible for disturbing Xiang and Hubei and coordinating with the Jiangxi Red Army to cause chaos in the Yangtze River area. He Jian, because Ye Kui had a few thousand party members lurking in the Changtan area, repeatedly induced him to confess the location of the hidden guns, but Ye refused to say anything. He ordered that Ye and Yi be tied to Liuyangmen outside the city and beheaded at 3 p.m. on the 26th. The heads were placed in wooden cages and taken to Lushan Town to be shown to the public. On that day, the crowd who went to the execution ground to watch was so large that it was congested. The Qingxiang Command Headquarters announced Ye Yi's crimes as follows: "For the announcement of the crimes, Ye Kui, the leader of the Communist Party, is a native of Lushanzhen, Changsha. He used to be the deputy chairman of the district agricultural association and was introduced by the chairman Yi Ziyi to join the Communist Party Xipi. His work was outstanding. After May and the Communist Kui Yi Lirong Teng Daiyuan incited him to organize a false peasant-worker revolutionary army, commanding bandits, destroying group offices, and carrying out burning and killing, plundering the Hexi area, and the disaster was extremely tragic. The Hunan Provincial Government offered a reward of 2,000 yuan for his arrest and the headquarters issued an arrest warrant, ordering the Changsha County Government to select teams and strictly arrest him without distinction. According to the county's teams and the Nanhua County teams, the bandit was arrested in Fuxingyuan in Huarong County. At the same time, Yi Shunding, the former pseudo secretary-general of the army and now the secretary of the special committee, and his accomplices Liu Zaisan and others, who conspired with the bandit Ye Kui to launch riots in Nanhua and Feng'an, were arrested. According to the county's orders, the bandit Ye Kui and Yi Shunding were presented to the department in advance. All the facts of the crime and the communist conspiracy to enter Changli from the border of Xiang and peep into Yue and E were confessed in court. In this way, the chief culprit was arrested, and the crime was unforgivable. He should be sentenced to death according to law to show a warning. In addition to signing and extracting the criminals Ye Kui and Yi Shunding, verifying their identity, tying them to the execution ground, and carrying out the death penalty, it is necessary to announce the crimes so that the public can know about it."

East Railway Solves Long-Standing Issues Meeting 78

Harbin dispatch on the 24th: The East Railway Board of Directors originally scheduled a joint meeting of directors and supervisors for 1:00 PM today. However, the Russian side claimed that the agenda was not adequately prepared and requested a one-day postponement. The meeting was rescheduled to 2:00 PM on the 25th with the agreement of the Chinese directors and supervisors. The Russian side's proposals for this meeting are mostly routine matters, while the Chinese side has approximately five items: (1) The concurrent use of Chinese and Russian languages in all railway agencies; (2) Demanding the return of detained carriages from the Ukrainian Railway; (3) Joint signing of official documents by Chinese and Russian heads of bureaus and departments; (4) Establishing a translation office within the Railway Bureau for translating documents between the two sides. The remaining item reportedly concerns budget issues. The two sides previously exchanged informal opinions several days ago. The Russian directors and supervisors expressed agreement with the Chinese proposals. It is expected that this meeting will not involve much dispute. Regarding the concurrent use of Chinese and Russian languages, the Chinese proposal explains that the predominance of Russian in the various departments of the Beijing Railway often causes difficulties in handling affairs. Furthermore, differences in language often lead to errors due to improper translation. In the future, every official document should have both a Chinese and Russian version, with each referencing the other's meaning. Chinese and Russian heads of bureaus and departments should jointly sign each document upon its promulgation. A separate translation office should be established under the Railway Bureau to handle this matter. Regarding the return of carriages detained by the Ukrainian Railway, the explanation states that after the Sino-Russian split, the Ukrainian Railway detained over 400 East Railway freight cars, 17 passenger cars, and 7 flatcars. As the East Railway is currently experiencing a period of booming transport, it is appropriate to return these carriages promptly. The other proposals also have attached explanations. However, even if the concurrent use of Chinese and Russian languages is passed by the Board of Directors, its implementation must still wait, partly because it is difficult to find translators in a short time, and partly because the railway budget must increase by at least 150,000 rubles per year.

Dispatch on the 26th: The East Railway Board of Directors meeting was successfully concluded yesterday afternoon. The proposals from both sides had been exchanged and read beforehand, and both sides agreed with each other, so the passage was quite easy. The important cases proposed by our side and passed by resolution include: (1) Concurrent use of Chinese and Russian languages, ordering the Railway Bureau to actively prepare and implement it in the shortest possible time, with Russian as the primary language and Chinese as the secondary language; (2) The name of the Central Library is inappropriate and should be changed to the China Eastern Railway Staff Library, and the scope should be reduced; (3) Various business institutions affiliated to the Railway Bureau should be merged and abolished in consideration of their wide range, and a committee should be organized immediately to review and implement commercialization; (4) The observation system is a matter within the scope of Chinese internal affairs and should be abolished immediately; (5) All Russian-detained vehicles after last year's incident should be ordered to be returned by the Railway Bureau immediately. The resolutions passed by the Russian side include: (1) Transferring Wang Zupei, Deputy Director of the Audit Bureau, to the Director of the General Affairs Office of the Board of Directors, and Zhang Mingzhe, Director of the General Affairs Office of the Railway Bureau, to Deputy Director of the Audit Bureau; (2) Replacing the Russian Chief Director Ge Jieer, and promoting Director Izmailov to fill the vacancy; (3) Due to the sharp rise in gold prices, formulating adjustment measures for railway freight and changing the exchange rate of Harbin silver dollars; (4) Extending the lease of the Gezhde East Railway Hotel for three years, until 1934.

First District Water Police Rescue Abducted Victims: He Yalin, captain of the First, Second, Third, and Fourth Squadrons of the First District Water Public Security Team, and others, previously received instructions from District Chief Chi to assemble forces to suppress bandits due to the rampant banditry. Zhang Yunfeng, Chief Inspector of the District Headquarters, was also ordered to lead warships to participate and bolster the forces. Change of Director of the Public Property Office: The previous director of the County Public Funds and Public Property Management Office resigned upon the expiration of his term, as he was not allowed to be reappointed according to regulations. Suzhou 80

Suzhou Municipal Government May Not Be Abolished: The Suzhou Municipal Government was ordered to be abolished, and Mayor Lu had previously ordered all bureaus and departments to handle the closure. Mayor Lu specially went to the province the day before yesterday to meet with Chairman Ye to ask for instructions on the aftermath of the municipal government's closure. After Chairman Ye invited Director Hu of the Civil Affairs Department to discuss the results, it was deemed that Suzhou City has a population of 260,000 in the 17th year and now the urban area has expanded and increased to more than 300,000. Therefore, it seems necessary to establish a city. As for the provincial government's monthly subsidy of 6,500 yuan, it must be for a period of three years. Therefore, Chairman Ye instructed Mayor Lu that the Suzhou Municipal Government should continue to work as usual, but the administrative expenses must be exceptionally frugal. Mayor Lu has returned to Suzhou and informed his subordinates to continue working as usual.

Actively Preparing for Price Stabilization: The price of rice in Suzhou has recently risen sharply, with the highest price rising to 17 yuan per stone, causing extreme panic among the common people. The Suzhou General Chamber of Commerce, in order to relieve the common people, sent a letter to the Wuxian Charity Granary on the 31st, urging them to expedite the handling of price stabilization. The Charity Granary is currently preparing to purchase grain, which is expected to be available in May. It is also known that the county and city will handle the price stabilization, with approximately 15,000 stones per month, calculated over three months, for a total of 45,000 stones. The granary currently has a stock of 90,000 stones of grain, which, after removing the rice husks, is suitable for the amount of 45,000 stones. As for the losses, they are approximately 300,000 yuan.

Gong Guoliang Ordered to Suppress Lake Bandits: Gong Guoliang, Director of the Third District of the Water Public Security Team, received an telegram from the Jiangsu Provincial Government on the 31st, stating that lake bandits in the Yangcheng Lake area on the border of Su and Kun are rampant. If they are not suppressed promptly, the situation will become uncontrollable. He was ordered to strictly supervise the suppression, etc. Director Gong immediately dispatched the Eleventh Squadron of the Water Public Security Team to suppress the bandits and immediately reported to the Provincial Government. It is also heard that Director Gong has a passive attitude and has submitted a report to the Provincial Government requesting approval to resign.

Large Band of Bandit Ships Discovered in Dayao: Yesterday (the 31st) at noon, more than 30 bandit ships arrived in Dayao, Suzhou (7-8 li from Chefang), fully equipped with guns and weapons. It is said that these bandit ships came from Luxu, Wujiang. After County Magistrate Huang of this area received a telegram from the Chexie District Office, he dispatched the Second Detachment of the First Squadron and the Third Detachment of the Third Squadron of the County Police to pursue and suppress them.

Kunshan 81

Military Police Launch Large-Scale Bandit Suppression: The banditry in Yangcheng Lake in the county is rampant, as repeatedly reported in this newspaper. Since the large band of lake bandits robbed the Tongli ferryboat near Zhaojiawan Town, the bandits retreated into Yangsantaimiao, at the junction of Wu, Kun, and Chang counties, where more than 200 bandit ships and three or four thousand lake bandits are entrenched, robbing ships and kidnapping people every day. Although the county police team has two squads stationed in Bacheng, they dare not advance due to their weak forces. The county government and the Party branch presented a report to the province requesting the dispatch of troops to suppress the bandits. On the 31st, the 28th Regiment of the Fifth Division of the stationed army was ordered to suppress the bandits. Regiment Commander Yao immediately ordered Battalion Commander Kuang to lead the entire battalion of soldiers with machine guns and mortars, transported by 20 ships towed by tugboats, to Bacheng. Li Guozhen, the captain of the Provincial Public Security Twelfth Squadron, also led patrol boat No. 20 to Bacheng. Subsequently, a telegram was sent to Changshu to join the county police team led by Captain Qian Wenyu to advance and suppress the bandits at 6:00 AM on the 31st.

Qingpu 82

Fierce Battle Between Police and Bandits Near Xicen: A small band of lake bandits arrived near Xicen, Qingpu, the day before yesterday, with more than 20 bandit ships and about 100 people, all equipped with guns and weapons. The water and land police team in Jinze heard the news and immediately went to suppress them. They encountered the bandits and engaged in a fierce battle for about three hours. The bandit forces were defeated and retreated towards the Mao River. It is said that three lake bandits were killed and four abducted victims were rescued. Two farmers were injured and killed by stray bullets. The water and land police team is currently pursuing and suppressing the bandits.

Water and Land Police Teams Jointly Suppress Lake Bandits: Lake bandits were discovered yesterday near Baitang, Jinze, Qingpu, with more than 100 bandit ships of various sizes and about 300 bandits. The county government, upon receiving the report, immediately ordered the county police team to dispatch a team to jointly suppress the bandits with the Second Squadron of the Water Public Security Team.

Resolution of Labor Dispute in the Pharmaceutical Industry: On March 15, employers in the local pharmaceutical industry dismissed more than ten employees. The dismissed workers reported to the labor union, requesting that it forward the report to higher authorities for negotiations. The union, based on the report, submitted a report to the county Party headquarters, requesting relief. The county Party headquarters, based on the report, convened a meeting of labor and management on the day before yesterday to mediate. As a result, Shi Yongshan and four others were given severance pay, while Chen Zaicheng and seven others were reinstated.

Large Numbers of Refugees Passing Through Looted Rice Boats: About 200 refugee boats from Lianshui County arrived in Baihejiang Town, Qingpu, at about 6:00 PM the day before yesterday, with more than 3,000 people, coming from Chonggu. The shops and residents were extremely frightened. Later, the district office raised 100 yuan to reward them, and they set sail towards Zhaotunqiao the next morning. It is also heard that they looted a rice boat along the way, causing considerable losses.

Wujiang 83

Bandit Ships Arrive Again in Luxu Town: Luxu Town, which suffered severe losses from a gang of bandits from Haizhou last winter, when more than 20 people were abducted, suddenly saw the arrival of more than 50 bandit ships yesterday (the 29th), anchored in Nanzha. There were more than 500 bandits, fully equipped with guns and cannons, all wearing symbols, looking like an army. After arriving in the town, they went ashore to shop, and there were no incidents of looting. 25th Regiment Dispatches Troops to Pingwang: Zhao Xiguang, the regimental commander of the 25th Regiment of the 13th Brigade of the Fifth Division stationed in Jiang, dispatched the First Battalion, the Second and Third Companies, to Pingwang yesterday (the 28th) due to the pervasive reeds in the four villages of the county. Wuxi 84

Measures to Relieve Rice Shortage: Zhao Zixin, the standing chairman of the local Rice and Bean Industry Association, recently stated that the price of rice has been rising daily (increasing to 16 yuan and 6 jiao per stone) without limit, putting the livelihoods of the common people in an increasingly precarious situation. If no measures are taken to provide relief, there are concerns about public security. The association drafted a letter of opinion and sent it to the joint association of rice industries in Ningbo and Shanghai counties and cities, proposing a general meeting to discuss and seek public opinion. They then submitted a petition to the Civil Affairs Department of the Provincial Government, requesting that it order the counties to convene local elders, start by raising funds, and purchase rice and grain separately. At the same time, they will use the accumulated grain and set up a bureau to stabilize prices in order to maintain the food supply for the people. The association also nominated Li Zhongchen, Huang Qixiang, and Ren Xunxian as representatives to go to Shanghai with Zhu Tuzheng, the representative of the rice milling industry, to discuss everything with the leaders of the rice industry in the north and south markets.

County Government Investigates Prison Break Case: Seven prisoners, including Li Chengguo, escaped from the local detention branch on the 25th late at night. It is now known that Zhou Cheng, a censor from the county government, signed in advance the transfer of Liu Yinqiu, the clerk of the branch, and prison guard Jiang Hailin and two other persons to the political police for detention. Zhou interrogated them in court. Liu and others gave vague testimony and shirked responsibility. Zhou believed that Liu Yinqiu was strongly suspected of accepting bribes to allow the prisoners to escape, and that the two prison guards, Jiang Hailin and others, had engaged in bribery and needed to be thoroughly investigated. He instructed that Liu Yinqiu and the two prison guards, Jiang Hailin and others, be sent to the prison to await a detailed report to the Higher Court for verification.

Preparing to Receive German Industrial Inspection Group: The German government, in order to investigate the industry and economic conditions of various provinces and counties in China, specially selected leaders from the German industrial and banking sectors with rich experience, including Lei Cimen, Haming, Huite, Luo Shengmeiqiu, Ji Kepei, Si Qiupeier, Kangtai, Tai Dingyusiluo, and Pei Ci, a total of ten people, and organized a German Industrial Inspection Group. Lei Cimen was appointed as the leader of the inspection group, leading the members to China by boat. The inspection group arrived in Hong Kong the day before yesterday to inspect the economy and industry. They are scheduled to travel from Hong Kong to Shanghai by boat on April 4 for inspection, and then go to Beijing on the 20th for investigation. They will spend a week inspecting in Beijing and then travel by train to Wuxi for inspection on the 28th. The Ministry of Agriculture and Mines of the National Government has received a telegram from the inspection group informing them of their arrival and is now preparing to receive them so that they can engage in hospitality at that time. The Ministry of Agriculture and Mines also dispatched Hu Boyuan, the director of the Mining Administration Department, by train to Wuxi yesterday afternoon to discuss reception matters with Rong Desheng, the leader of the flour mill, and Chen Zhanru, the acting chairman of the county chamber of commerce. He then returned to Beijing in the evening. At the same time, the county chamber of commerce also received an official letter from the Ministry of Agriculture and Mines, informing them to prepare for the reception. After receiving the letter, the association immediately sent letters to the four groups of silk yarn, flour, and money, requesting them to properly entertain the inspection group upon their arrival in Wuxi.

Autopsy Record of Songshan Murder Case: Gu Jinbiao, a worker at the Yongli Stone Mining Company in Songshan Xiayongli Stone Mining Company, Tusi Village 432, Beishang Township, County has recently been reported missing. It was not until the day before yesterday that Gu's body was found in Songshan River. Later, the Township Police Team arrested two suspects, Tang Shouxin and Xu Guirong, (both workers at Yongli Stone Mining Company) and escorted them to the county for interrogation. It is now known that Yu, an investigating censor, went to the countryside to conduct an autopsy at 8:00 AM yesterday. It was discovered that the deceased Gu Jinbiao had been stopped from working by the chief foreman Wang Zhizhen on the 24th of this month. At the same time, Tang Shouxin was also stopped from working. Gu Jinbiao went missing on the 25th after being suspended, and the body was not found in Songshan River until the day before yesterday. After the investigating censor Yu completed the investigation, he immediately ordered the coroner Shen to conduct an autopsy according to law. The autopsy determined that he had fallen into the river and drowned before death. After the autopsy, he instructed the Yongli Stone Mining Company to prepare a coffin for burial. Yu also considered that Wang Zhizhen, the chief foreman of the company, had suspicions of coercion, so he took Wang to the city for interrogation.

Deputy Township Chief Makes False Accusation out of Spite: Fei Zhongliang, the deputy township chief of Shangxing Lane, Xishui Township, Kaiyuan Township, County had accumulated grievances with Gao Zhongyu, a fellow villager. Yesterday, he reported to the Ninth Sub-bureau of the Public Security Bureau that Gao Zhongyu had engaged in communist activities, holding secret meetings at home every night and posting slogans. After receiving the report, Bureau Chief Lu dispatched a patrol officer with the plaintiff Fei Zhongliang to search Gao Zhongyu's house. Upon arriving at Gao's house, they found no activity and only took Gao Zhongyu to the bureau. After Bureau Chief Lu opened a court for preliminary interrogation, Gao Zhongyu stated that Fei Zhongliang had falsely accused him of being a communist due to accumulated grievances. Lu believed that the case involved false accusation out of spite and immediately prepared a document to send the plaintiff and defendant to the Public Security Bureau for transfer to the county government for interrogation.

Thieves Apprehended in Two Homicide and Theft Cases: Fang Guangjin's house in Xizhatou, Zhengluqiao, Wuyi County, was stolen and robbed on the evening of the 4th of this month. Changshu 86

Qingyang Ferry Returns Due to Bandit Reports: The Qingyanggang ferry sailed from Changshu to Kunshan on the morning of the 29th. At about 10 o'clock, when it arrived in the Nanhuangjing area, it saw ships traveling to Shanghai ahead of it turning back, claiming that there were several bandit ships in the Beiqiao area, intercepting rice boats. It was also heard that the refugees on the shore were mixed with the bandit ships and had robbed a rice boat. The passengers of the ship requested the accountant to turn the ship back. At noon, the local Public Security Bureau also received this information and immediately telegraphed the county government, which ordered Qian Wenyu, the captain of the police team, to go to the countryside for investigation. The Public Security Bureau immediately convened an emergency meeting of all sub-stations in the urban area and ordered martial law.

County Magistrate Pang Scheduled to Take Office in Kunshan: After the Provincial Civil Affairs Department announced the transfer of Pang Shusen, the county magistrate of this county, to Kunshan County, Wu, the county magistrate of Kunshan, went to Danyang the week before to take office. County Magistrate Pang then received an order from the Department to take office in Kunshan immediately. As for the issue of the new county magistrate Tan Yigui coming to Changshu, he is serving as a secretary in the Civil Affairs Department and will postpone his arrival in Changshu. It is now known that County Magistrate Pang is scheduled to take office in Kunshan on April 1.

Nantong 87

Bandits Captured and Escorted for County Trial: Military police in the eastern countryside suppressed bandits and captured 11 bandits, including Chen Xiaobing, seizing amulets, weapons, and ammunition. On the 29th, after interrogation by the county government, they were all imprisoned. In addition, Zhu Wu, the director of the Public Security Sub-bureau of the Sanyi District, was arrested for colluding with bandits and escorted to the city that night. After County Magistrate Chen returns to the city from the eastern countryside, he will personally interrogate him and temporarily detain him in the detention center.

Naval Staff Officer Transferred to Commander: Liu Huanqian, a staff officer of the Naval Training Fleet, led the Marine Corps in Nantong to suppress bandits. On the 29th, he was transferred to the commander of the Weisheng warship by order of the Ministry of the Navy. Ye Jinqin was appointed to fill the vacancy. Liu went to Gaochangmiao, Shanghai that night to take over the job. The team in Nantong was reorganized under the command of Liu Xiaojun, the deputy commander of the Yingrui warship.

Lusi Sea Bandits Harass Extensively: Lusi Sanjiaozhen has recently been occupied by sea bandits, who are kidnapping and extorting ransoms, forcing fishermen to pay fees and obtain flags, burning ships and killing people in nearby villages and towns, almost every night. Merchants and residents in the northeast have moved away completely. Gunshots can be heard all night in Lusi Town. The district office sent people to the city to ask the county government to quickly dispatch a team for support.

Zhenjiang 88

Automobile Accident Caused by Jiangsu Construction Department: At about 12:00 PM yesterday, a Jiangsu Provincial Construction Department's No. 997 truck carrying cement pipes from Paiwan was driving on the slope of Jingji Ridge when two rickshaws were coming down the hill. Due to inadequate avoidance, the front rickshaw was overturned, breaking the shaft, and the rickshaw puller's leg was slightly injured. The rear wheel then injured the face of an elderly woman named Chen Zhong, who was over sixty years old, causing her to bleed profusely and lose consciousness. Her son and personnel from the Seventh Sub-bureau of the section carried her to the Provincial Hospital for treatment. However, due to her old age and weakness and excessive bleeding, she died in the hospital at about 9:00 PM in the evening. The Seventh Sub-bureau has transferred the driver of the accident, Min Asi, to the court for punishment.

Provincial Police Team Busy Suppressing Bandits: Li Ziya, the captain of the special service team of the Jiangsu Provincial Police Corps, was ordered by Captain Li yesterday to go to Tongzhou to suppress bandits. After receiving the order, the captain led the team by boat yesterday. In addition, Yu Shimei, the captain of the Fourth Brigade of the Jiangsu Police Corps, was ordered to go to Liyang to suppress bandits. Now that the bandits have been cleared, the team led all the soldiers back to the province by boat yesterday.

Fuyun Fengyun Ferry Sinks: At about 10:00 AM yesterday, the Fuyun Company's Fengyun ferry collided with a grain boat at Guazhoukou. The front of the ferry was caught by the planks of the grain boat, immediately opening a hole. It sank in less than ten minutes. The passengers on board, seeing the accident, avoided it by boarding a tugboat, so no one was injured.

Yangzhou 89

Telegram Requesting Troops to Nantong to Suppress Bandits: Zhang Jiarui, the Huaiyun envoy, reported that Yuan Desheng, the chief of the Tongzhou General Salt Field, said in his fast mail that bandits are rampant in the lower river area, disrupting the people and salt workers of the fields, and even kidnapping people for ransom, requesting that he transfer the matter to the Salt Office to dispatch troops to severely suppress them. Yesterday (the 28th), in addition to approving the transfer to the Salt Office, requesting the dispatch of troops to jointly suppress the bandits with the Provincial Public Security Bureau brigade in order to eliminate them, he also ordered the field offices to direct the land and water anti-smuggling camps stationed in various places to block and suppress them as appropriate.

Guijiang Ten Dams Sag and Collapse in Three Places: The Grand Canal north of the Yangtze River has Guijiang Ten Dams. Recently, the spring floods have been gradually rising. Yesterday (the 29th), the Canal Engineering Office repeatedly received reports from the dam committees stating that Xinba, Tushanluo, and Fenghuang Dam had sagged and collapsed one after another, and were about to collapse, adding that Tushan Dam was the most dangerous of the three dams. The Engineering Office's Director Shan ordered Zhang Shuyuan and others, the people in charge of repairing the dams, to go to various places to find ways to save them.

Jiaxing 90

Appeal Prisoner Escapes by Jumping from Train: A county Public Security Bureau inspection officer at Jiaxing Station seized a large sum of banknotes from a passenger named Wang Ziming last month, including a word strip indicating the sale of opium, suspecting him of selling opium. The county bureau sent him to court for interrogation. As a result, Wang Ziming was sentenced to three years and six months of imprisonment and fined. Wang filed an appeal against the verdict, so the police were dispatched to escort him to the Hangzhou Higher Court a few days ago. When the train passed Linping, Wang jumped from the train and escaped. The bailiff was unable to pursue him and also fled after arriving in Hangzhou.

Pinghu 91

Defeated Bandits Scatter and Loot: The large gang of bandits in Lexiang was bravely and painfully suppressed by the provincial security team, and the bandits were scattered. A few days ago, two small leaders were captured and beheaded by the Jiangsu Water Police. The bandits then scattered in the countryside, looting everywhere. It is estimated that on the night of the 23rd, eight houses were looted in a row in Leyiqiehe Tangjiaqiaobei, Yaqian, Lexiang. On the night of the 24th, three or four houses were looted in the countryside at Qiqandi. On the night of the 25th, Zhang Fusheng's house in Nanfanggang was robbed. On the night of the 26th, Zhang Jinsheng's house near Yaqian was also robbed, causing considerable losses.

Xiaoshan 92

Kidnapper Captured Twice: Gao Meisheng, a notorious ruffian in Nanyang, Dongxiang, Xiaoshan, colluded with kidnappers to abduct his nephew Wang (from Toupeng) in 1926 and demand a ransom. He was captured by the county government and sentenced to 13 years of imprisonment. Later, a lawyer appeared on the scene to appeal on his behalf, reducing the sentence to 10 years. He was released on bail in January of this year. However, the case still required 600 yuan. Gao, being cunning by nature, ignored it after being released. Therefore, he was reported this time and arrested repeatedly. Gao had already heard the news and absconded to avoid arrest. On the 27th, Gao came to the city for some reason and was spotted by a bailiff from the county court, who captured him and escorted him to the court.

Incense Boat Robbed En Route: On the night of the 29th, two incense boats sailing from Shaoxing to the Laoyue Temple in Xiaoshan were suddenly stopped by three bandit ships with more than ten bandits near Qianqing and Yangfanqiao. The bandits boarded the ship and robbed all the pilgrims of their gold and silver jewelry, cotton quilts, and clothes, worth three or four hundred gold in total. They also cut the boatman Miao Kui in two places on his leg.
