Shen Bao Education News

National Games Special Issue (No. 1)

Sensational Opening of National Games 93

Opening Ceremony Held at 9:00 AM This Morning

Chairman Chiang to Attend and Deliver Speech

Competitions Begin and Continue for Ten Days

Two Thousand Athletes Display Their Skills

The sensational National Games will open at the Donggaoqiao Daying venue in Hangzhou at 9:00 AM this morning. The venue's magnificent architecture and complete layout are unprecedented in our country. Chairman Chiang of the National Government will attend the ceremony and deliver a training speech. The president and vice presidents, represented by Shi Weihuan, Zhu Jiahua, the director of the preparatory committee, Zhou Xiangxian and Huang Mingdao, the deputy directors, and committee members of various departments and staff members of various groups, are scheduled to attend the meeting at 7:00 AM this morning. Representatives from various agencies and organizations, as well as school military police guests, are expected to number tens of thousands. The situation yesterday is recorded below:

Introduction (Chong Gan) 94

The grand and magnificent National Games have opened in Hangzhou today. Two thousand of the nation's outstanding male and female athletes have gathered on the shores of West Lake, each showcasing their fine skills. This is truly an unprecedented grand event. Who dares say that our nation lacks a spirit of martial valor?

The purpose of holding the Games is to promote national physical education. It coincides with the Ninth Far Eastern Games, to be held in Japan in May of this year. This is an opportunity to select outstanding performers to attend the Games in Japan, to win glory for our country.

This Games has many unique features. Here are a few points:

1. The Games are being held based on a government resolution, and various provinces and cities have followed suit, first holding preliminary rounds. The public enthusiastically participated, selecting representatives to compete in Hangzhou. This demonstrates the spirit of cooperation among the people of the whole country.

2. In the past, athletes were all students, with participation lacking from government, business, and industrial circles. Recently, there has been considerable effort to promote amateur sports. Those participating in the Games include people from all walks of life. This demonstrates the popularization of sports nationwide.

3. In our country, women have traditionally been considered beautiful for being delicate and refined, and not venturing far from home was the norm. But now, a generation of robust, short-clothed, leg-revealing, and athletically beautiful women are gallantly racing on the sports field. Even from the remote Northeast and Southwest, they have not shied away from the arduous journey, all coming to compete. This shows that physical education in our country has become widespread among women.

In addition, the reporter feels compelled to say a few words to those in charge and to the athletes, on three points:

1. The Games have sufficient talent and are well-funded. The preparatory procedures have been meticulously organized. The competitions will commence today and are certain to proceed smoothly. However, this grand event must not be a fleeting moment of glory. Once the competitions are over, it should not be relegated to the past. It is hoped that our leaders will allocate dedicated funds annually to promote national public physical education. Taking advantage of this gathering of physical education experts, they should plan appropriate methods for promoting physical education, to strengthen the foundation of our nation. How can this be neglected?

2. Athletes participating in the competitions should certainly strive for top rankings and excellent results. However, they should also embrace a spirit of "benevolence and chivalry," adhere to the rules of sportsmanship, and obey the referees' decisions. Better to lose a championship than to compromise morality.

3. Those participating in this Games all possess considerable ability and physical strength, and have had more opportunities to train with foreigners. They have a relatively strong chance of winning. However, they must not become arrogant because of this. Those athletes with lesser results may be that way due to their physical condition or lack of training opportunities. They should not be discouraged. The purpose of holding the Games is to promote physical education. Trophies are merely objects of encouragement. Being able to participate in the Games already makes one an athletic champion. This newspaper is dedicated to promoting physical education and will spare no effort. This National

Games should be extensively publicized. We wish the Games success and offer our humble contributions, hoping they will be accepted by all involved in the Games.

The Significance of the Games (Zhu Jia-hua) 95

In this season of bright spring colors, the National Games, which have been prepared for months, have finally opened on the splendid shores of West Lake. What a joyful and heartening event!

Our country has long been ridiculed by the great powers as the "Sick Man of East Asia." This is undeniable. Just look at how few of our country's youth are not thin and weak, barely able to support their clothes. If the youth are like this, there is no need to mention the others. If we were to compare our country's citizens with those of the great powers, we would immediately feel "inferior." The great powers call us sick men, which is indeed a form of mockery, but it also provides us with valuable criticism. We should know that to have a sound mind, we must first have a sound body. Only by uniting millions of citizens with sound bodies can we create a healthy nation. Only a healthy nation can create a healthy culture. The Chinese nation is inherently a nation rich in creative spirit. However, the weakness of the scholarly style has persisted through the ages, causing the nation's physical education to decline day by day. This has affected the spirit of the entire nation, leading to a state of complacency, and the inherent creative abilities have been almost completely lost. In recent years, due to contact with other

Important Officials of the Games 96

(1) Honorary Chairman: Chiang Kai-shek, (2) Chairman: Dai Jitao, (3) Vice Chairman: Zhang Jingjiang, (4) Vice Chairman: He Yingqin, (5) Director of Preparation: Zhu Jiahua, (6) Secretary-General: Ma Xun

(Photo courtesy of Guanghua Studio, Nanjing)

strong and healthy nations, and the pressure they have exerted, we have come to realize the reasons for our country's weakness. The most significant reason is the weakness of the national physique. Therefore, the issue of physical education has gradually attracted the attention of the Chinese people. In the newspapers of commercial cities, we can see news about sports competitions every day. As for the National Games, it has been held two or three times in the past. Now, the public's interest in physical education and sports is growing continuously. Therefore, this Games will certainly exert a more profound and extensive significance than the previous ones.

We believe that the first point worth recognizing about the significance of this Games is that it was decided by the central government. The central government's decision to hold this Games has two meanings. First, the targets of the domestic revolution, the warlords, have now been almost completely destroyed by the revolutionary forces. From now on, the direction of the revolution must shift outwards. In other words, we must implement the task of overthrowing imperialism. However, the defenses of imperialism are deep and strong, not as easily destroyed as the domestic warlords. To overthrow imperialism, we must have adequate preparation. Otherwise, even if we shout slogans of overthrowing imperialism every day, it will be useless. Setting aside other matters, let's first talk about the physique of our citizens. If we are all like sick men, struggling to even lift a gun with both hands, then trying to resist the warriors of the great powers with these sick men would be truly overestimating ourselves. Therefore, to overthrow imperialism, we must start by strengthening the physique of our citizens. Second, we have now reached the most important stage of the period of political tutelage, which is construction. However, after a society or country has undergone significant destruction, rebuilding a new society or country is an arduous task. This arduous task cannot be shouldered by a declining nation. Therefore, all Chinese citizens should know that we must strive for "revolution" and strive for physical education, strive for "construction" and strive for physical education.

The second point worth noting is the method of selecting athletes for this Games, which is different from previous years. In the past, the method of producing athletes from the East China, South China, North China, West China, and Central China regional games was used. This time, provinces, special municipalities, and overseas Chinese groups are used as units. The reason for changing to this method is to enable all athletes in the country, under the leadership and encouragement of the government, to be generally mobilized. We believe that in this meeting, many new athletes from various places will definitely be discovered, and they will create surprising records. We also hope that everyone will follow suit and that people's sports meets, amateur sports meets, etc., will be held continuously.

In the past, general athletes had a kind of mistaken idea, which was "to engage in sports for the sake of sports" or "to engage in sports for the sake of trophies." Saying "to engage in sports for the sake of sports" is as meaningless as saying "to eat for the sake of eating, to read for the sake of reading." Saying "to engage in sports for the sake of trophies" is even more ridiculous, just like saying "to read for the sake of exams, to read for the sake of a graduation diploma." The purpose of sports, to put it narrowly, is to seek the development of individual physical education. However, individuals cannot exist apart from society, so further, in addition to seeking the development of individual physical education, we must also seek the development of the physical education of the entire society. We hope that the athletes who come to this meeting can completely break the mistaken ideas of the past and understand that the purpose of this meeting is to develop national physical education and invigorate the spirit of the nation.

A Brief History of the National Games 97

The National Games was founded in the second year of the reign of Emperor Xuantong of the Qing Dynasty. More than twenty years have passed since then, and three Games have been held successively. The first Games was held in the second year of Xuantong (1911 AD) in the Nanyang Industrial Exposition in Nanjing. The second Games was held in the third year of the Republic of China, that is, 1914 AD, in the Temple of Heaven in Beijing. The participating teams, sports events, and scoring methods of these two Games were not in accordance with legal regulations. Even the officials in the Games were mostly Westerners. At that time, there were still few Chinese people engaged in physical education, and their knowledge and experience were limited. The facilities and preparations for the Games had to rely heavily on Westerners. It was not until the third Games was held in Wuchang in the thirteenth year of the Republic of China that there was a formal organization. All rules were in accordance with those stipulated by the Far Eastern Games. Therefore, the formal National Games should begin with the third Games. Before the seventh and eighth Far Eastern Games, our country held national preliminary rounds to select representatives to attend the Games. The scale was grand and the event was extremely prosperous. However, there were only three officially named National Games.

The National Sports Advancement Association's board of directors decided two years ago to hold the fourth National Games in Guangzhou in October of last year. At the same time, the Zhejiang Provincial Government also initiated the National Games. Therefore, the Games in Guangzhou last year was canceled, and today's grand meeting in West Lake was held.

The Process of Preparation 98

The National Games has been prevalent in European and American countries for more than just a day or two. In our country, due to political instability and frequent unrest, there has been no time for this great plan. This is deeply regrettable. Since the establishment of our National Government, construction has been the most urgent task. Because of the stagnation of industry, the West Lake Exposition was created to promote industry and commerce. After four months, the results were remarkable. Furthermore, because the prosperity and decline of national undertakings are always tied to the growth and decline of talent, in order to promote national physical education and promote the spirit of the nation, the National Games is being held.

(1) Appointment of Officials 99

The National Games was produced based on the decision passed by the 197th meeting of the Central Political Conference. It was decided to be held in Hangzhou City, Zhejiang Province, starting on April 1, 19. At the same time, Chiang Chung-cheng, Chairman of the National Government, was appointed as Honorary Chairman of the Games, Dai Chuanxian as Chairman, Zhang Renjie and He Yingqin as Vice Chairmen, and Zhu Jiahua as Director of Preparation. In addition, the Chairman appointed Zhou Xiangxian and Huang Mingdao as Deputy Directors of Preparation, and Ma Xun as Secretary-General. The Preparatory Office was established on September 25, 18, initially attached to the Zizhi Vocational School on Mapo Lane in Hangzhou, and began preparations. An accounting section was established, and Shu Hong was appointed as a clerk to manage it. Zhu Yaoting was appointed as a clerk to manage the engineering section, Wu Zhuozhi was appointed as a clerk to manage the administrative section, Wu Bangwei was appointed as a clerk to manage the competition section, and Yu Jimin was appointed as a clerk to manage the security section. A document accounting team was also established to assist. This is the situation of the organization.

(2) Financial Situation 100

This Games is an initiative in our country. Its fame has spread widely, and people from all over the country are vying to witness this grand event. Even countries around the world are eagerly anticipating it. Furthermore, given the attention of foreigners, it is especially important to strive for perfection. When the central government made its decision, the original budget was set at 260,000. The Zhejiang Provincial Government Committee decided to allocate 100,000, Jiangsu 10,000, Guangdong 10,000, Hubei 10,000, Anhui 3,000, Jiangxi 3,000, Shanghai Special Municipality 3,000, Guizhou 2,000, Liaoning 1,000, and Heilongjiang 500, for a total of 142,500. Compared to the original amount, there is still a shortage of more than 100,000. This is the financial situation.

(3) Construction of the Venue 101

The competitions in the Games include all outdoor sports in the Far Eastern Games. To hold various sports in the same venue, the selection of the venue was extremely difficult. Initially, the training ground of Jianqiao was selected. Later, because it was too far from the city and inconvenient for transportation, it was decided to hold it at the Meidong Gaoqiao Dayingpan. The site was originally the garrison of the Sixth Division Engineering Battalion and the headquarters of the Third Regiment of the Security Team. As a result of the negotiations for relocation, the eastern and central parts of the camp remained for the use of the battalion, and the western houses and club were ceded for the use of the Games office. This is the situation of the venue and the buildings.

The venue covers an area of ​​approximately 300 acres, with a track and field stadium, running track, football field, basketball court, tennis court, and baseball field. Contractors were invited to bid. The design and drawing were the responsibility of the design and engineering sections. The bidding was decided on October 18th, and seven construction factories, including Xie Shun, were selected to build the venue. The original plan was for three months of design and three months of construction. However, since the beginning of last winter, there has been continuous rain and snow, totaling more than 80 days of rain and snow during the construction period. Therefore, the design period was shortened, and the construction period was extended to four months. From March 1st, as the opening of the Games approached, workers were added every day, always more than 700 people. Sometimes construction was still carried out at night. Therefore, this great project was successfully completed in the shortest possible time. The original gate in the venue was in disrepair due to age. The surrounding walls were also mottled and dilapidated. The gaps in the shade of the walls were filled with piles of tiles. In addition to repairing the gates and side doors to make them tall, solemn, and beautiful, several convenient doors were added in the four corners for entry and exit. The entire venue was leveled and fenced with bamboo fences to maintain order. For the convenience of visitors, many bleachers were built in the style of sports fields in various countries. They are spacious and comfortable and can accommodate 10,000 people. As for the command platform, it must be able to command the entire venue. It was carefully structured based on the style of the National Games in Europe and the United States, combined with the advantages of our country's inherent architecture. It is three lengths long and two lengths wide, and its height is sufficient to hold more than 200 people. During the construction, five pillars were required to support it. Once completed, all five pillars were removed so as not to obstruct the view of the audience. The point of support was based on Fang Xue. However, due to the lack of space in the venue, the swimming pool was held at the swimming pool of Zhijiang University. By March 15th, all projects had been completed, and only needed to be tidied up and painted before they could be arranged. However, from the 16th to the 18th, the provincial games were held, and construction had to be stopped. After a meeting of officials, it was decided that the construction would be fully completed on March 25th. This is the situation of the project.

(4) Preparation for Hospitality 102

This Games brings together athletes from all over the country. Overseas Chinese compatriots will also participate in the Games. It is estimated that there will be no fewer than 2,000 athletes. The preparation of dormitories and food was also very difficult. Wu Zhuozhi, Director of Administrative Affairs, Hua Dong Baseball Team

(Photograph courtesy of China)

worked hard to plan. The western part of the barracks was repaired to provide accommodation for male athletes. More than 2,000 beds were rushed to be made. A large dining hall was built on top of the empty barracks. Bathrooms and toilets are fully equipped in the dormitory. The dining hall can accommodate 300 seats, and the air is spacious and hygienic. Female athletes will stay at the West Lake Villa as a residence. In order to treat athletes from afar, the Ministry of Railways, the Shipping Association, the China Merchants Bureau, and the Dalian Jinyi Company were specifically requested to charge all participating athletes half price. They were all approved. The Administrative Affairs Section prepared half-price certificates and sent them to various provinces and cities for distribution at the time. The China Travel Service was entrusted to provide hospitality and guidance in various places. Hospitality stations were set up at Hangzhou and Shanghai railway stations to guide visitors. The planning was thorough and meticulous.

Guangdong Women's Basketball Team

(Photograph courtesy of China)

(5) Drafting of the Emblem 103

The Games' opening, the distribution of free entry tickets to schools and organizations for visits, and the sale of tickets to other visitors for a fee were all restricted. All officials serving in the Games were issued official badges for identification. Appointed committee members and consultants were given committee badges. In addition, athletes were given athlete badges.

The emblem of this association was also submitted to the chairman for approval. The style is. There are five beams on the outside, symbolizing the five continents. There are 36 teeth inside, representing 36 groups. The three colors of red, blue, and white symbolize the blue sky, white sun, and red earth. The wavy line below indicates the Qiantang River tide. All kinds of badges are based on the emblem. In order to commemorate the Games and express its long-term significance, a calendar was specially printed. The emblem is listed on it. In the middle is the inscription of Zhang Jingjiang, Chairman of the Zhejiang Provincial Government, a key figure in the party and the country. The brushwork is strong, and the momentum is full. It is a work of the year.

(6) Expanding Publicity 104

The fame of the Games has spread throughout the country. In order to expand publicity, the Administrative Affairs Section specifically set up a publicity team to edit all publications, disseminate news messages, and design advertising matters. Wu Jianying was specially appointed as the team leader, and Xu Tailai, a reporter from Hangzhou, and others were appointed to assist him. From February 16th, news about the preparations was compiled and published nationwide every day. Wu Jianying also compiled a large book of abstracts to report the situation of the Preparatory Office and various regulations, so that the audience could follow the instructions. After the Games opened, a daily newspaper was compiled and printed every day to report the situation in the venue. Stores are necessary in the venue. Many houses were specially built for rent. The rent was kept low to show consideration for the difficulties of merchants. All of these are the preparation of the Administrative Affairs Section.

(7) Enthusiastic Participation 105

All 36 groups from provinces and cities across the country participated in the Games. The competition trophies were set at 12, including 8 for men and 4 for women, all based on the Far Eastern Games. A committee of 13 was established under the Competition Section to manage all competition affairs of the Games. As for the various competition regulations, they were all formulated by Wu Bangwei, clerk of the Competition Section, as the standard. This is the preparation situation of the competition.

Statistics from the beginning of the preparation to the opening are only half a year. All venue projects and various affairs have been completed without any omissions. If it were not for the enthusiasm and mission of the Director of Preparation and the hard work of the personnel of each section, it would be difficult to achieve this result. Therefore, the process of preparation is described to the readers.

Venue Layout

Bird's-Eye View of the Venue 106

The venue of the Games is located at Meidong Gaoqiao Dayingpan in Hangzhou, which was originally a garrison. It is close to the city and has convenient transportation. It covers an area of ​​approximately 300 acres. To the north is the Games Preparatory Office. In addition to various offices, there is a temporary bank for the convenience of athletes to deposit and exchange money. To the north of the square, in the middle is the dormitory for female athletes, and to the west is the dormitory for male athletes. In the southwest is a temporary dining hall that can accommodate more than 300 seats. In the southeast corner is a consumer cooperative. In front of the Preparatory Office, across a wide road, is the Games venue, surrounded by walls. The walls are covered with paintings and slogans, which make people feel excited. The gate is especially grand and solemn. Inside, bamboo fences are used for separation, which is full of variety. Every place has an emblem and guide lines, which are divided into a track and field stadium, running track, football field, basketball court, tennis court, and baseball field. There are many bleachers, which can accommodate 10,000 people. Simple houses are built on the edge of the field for commercial rental and sales. The command platform is located in the western part of the venue, overlooking the entire field, so it is convenient for command. In addition, the swimming pool is located in the mountain depression of Zhijiang University. The clear spring water is灌　and is especially hygienic.

Track and Field Stadium 107

The track and field stadium is located on the far west side of the Games venue. There has been sufficient preparation in advance, so the equipment is quite complete. The command platform in the center of the west side of the stadium is in a straight line with the bleachers. At the west end of the stadium, there are several temporary rest rooms for athletes, which are the rest areas for male and female athletes. A white flagpole is erected in the center of the stadium. Flags of various countries are hung on all sides. The flags of the party and the country and the flag of the Games are fully inserted around the stadium. They are fluttering in the wind, shining brightly, and adding a lot of color to the venue. The most noteworthy thing is the wooden railing around the track, which is three feet high. Every ten feet or so, there is a partition with a number on it, which is said to be convenient for groups to visit and investigate, and to maintain order and safety. Although the matter is extremely minor, it can be said that the designer has racked his brains and is meticulous. During the Games, spectators enter and exit from one　in the northwest corner of the stadium.

Football Field 108

The football field is on the left side of the track and field stadium, only separated by a fence. The length of the field is about 120 yards, and the width is about 70 yards, which is quite appropriate in size. The bleachers around the field can accommodate three or four thousand people. The entrance and exit are from the main gate on the south side of the field. Short railings are installed around the field to prevent spectators from rushing in. However, due to time constraints, the land has not been laid with grass, only sand and mud.

Basketball and Volleyball Courts 109

There is one basketball court and two volleyball courts, which are adjacent to each other. Bamboo fences are used as walls, covering an area of ​​more than ten acres. The basketball court is made of wooden boards, one foot above the ground, and painted red. It is more than one hundred and ten feet long and more than seventy feet wide. The blue frames are painted blue and stand upright outside the court. The white blue boards extend into the court by about seven feet. The construction is quite strong. The boundary lines of the ball court are black, and the red and black are not very clear. The court is surrounded by a three-foot-high railing to prevent spectators from entering. There are bleachers on the east, south, and west sides, which can accommodate more than a thousand spectators. In the middle of the bleachers on the west side is the seat for news reporters and guests. The scoreboard is on top of the reporter's seat, which is the highest point in the entire field. The audience can see the score of the game at a glance. To the west of the basketball court is the volleyball court. The two courts are connected to each other and can allow four teams to play at the same time. The ground is covered with grass, and the bleachers are on the east and west sides, with the same layout as the basketball court. Basketball and volleyball players enter and exit from the main gate on the north side. There are small gates in all four corners, and players can exit from the small gates after the game.

Tennis Court 110

The tennis court is in the southeast corner, with entry and exit from the main gate on the south side. It covers an area of ​​six or seven acres and is separated from other courts by bamboo fences. The five tennis courts are arranged in a row, paved with yellow sand, which is smooth and beautiful. The southwest and east sides are bleachers. The south bleachers are about seven feet above the ground and can accommodate more than 1,500 people. There are also small gates in all four corners, which can connect to various courts.

Baseball Field 111

The baseball field is located in the northeast of the Games venue. The field is vast, and there is only one row of bleachers on the north side. The layout is relatively simple. The outer field is a grass field, and the inner field is paved with fine coal cinder to prevent it from being slippery after rain. There are small gates on the southwest and west sides, which can connect to the basketball and volleyball courts.

Swimming Pool 112

The All-China Games swimming pool, due to the temporary inability to construct a suitable swimming pool at the venue, has been decided to be used in conjunction with the pool at Jiang University at Erlongtou, Jianggan. As a reporter, seeing that sports are being actively promoted in China and thus are receiving national attention, I personally went to observe it. The findings are detailed below for the reference of my most admired swimming comrades and visitors from all directions. (A) "Location": This pool is located on the hillside of Erlongtou in Jianggan, facing the Qiantang River. To the left is the Ya Peak of Baopu, and to the right are the dormitories of Jiang University. Behind the pool and high above is the gymnasium under construction. The surrounding area is full of jagged rocks, bamboo, trees, flowers, and grass. The pavilion nestled among the Baopu Peaks adds a touch of tranquility, making my heart feel even more at ease. In relation to West Lake, the pool is located to the southwest; in relation to the Qiantang River, it is located to the northeast. (B) "Construction": The pool's construction began in the spring of 1927 (the 16th year of the Republic of China) and took about half a year to complete. The total construction cost from start to finish was approximately 5,000 yuan. The perimeter of the pool is made of reinforced concrete, with an iron pipe at each corner. On the southwest side of the pool's bottom, there is an outlet for draining water. The pool is surrounded by stone railings and distributed stone benches, unlike other places with glass awnings, which is to follow the natural trend. The bottom of the pool was originally carved from mountain rocks, giving it a unique architectural beauty. (C) "Water Source": The water used in the swimming pool is critical to the health of the swimmers and should be carefully considered. When the pool was first built, it was intended to mechanically draw water from the Qiantang River. However, after repeated tests by engineers, it was found that the river water not only had excessive salinity but also contained other unsanitary substances. Therefore, it was changed to use mountain spring water, drawn from the streams and ravines of the mountain through pipes into the pool. The water is warm, heavy, and exceptionally clean. (D) "Plans": After inspecting the pool, the reporter asked Mr. He Weicong, the Dean of Jiang University, if there were any other improvement plans. Mr. He said that he had long planned to carve the mountain walls on the left, right, and back of the pool into natural chair-like seats, so that those who are fascinated by swimming could have a comfortable place to sit and fulfill their desire to watch swimming. However, it is currently limited by funding, but he hopes to start construction in the near future. He added that it is a pity that this pool is being used for the All-China Games. The improvement of this pool is what I hope for, and I hope that the education authorities can make further efforts to construct more pools, so that new Chinese swimmers can have a place to show their skills. (E) "Transportation": The location of the swimming pool is about seven li from the entrance of the All-China Games. There are buses of the Gongsan section of the Zhejiang Provincial Highway Bureau that can connect it. Other means of transportation, such as private cars and rickshaws, can also be used. Going west along the pool's front leads to Fuyang County; going east leads to Zhakou, where you can cross the river to Xixing. Climbing the mountain behind the pool, you can see the gentle and lovely West Lake.

Actual Number of Registrations 115

A total of 22 provinces and cities

More than 2,000 athletes

Hangzhou Electric Report, 31st – The unprecedented All-China Games, after a long period of full preparation, opened this morning. As of last night, the actual number of registered groups, counted by unit, was 22 provinces and cities, with a total of more than 2,000 people, of which athletes account for more than one-fifth. Gathering from the north and south is truly a grand occasion. Combined with the famous West Lake, it adds more color to the beautiful scenery and this grand event. Moreover, the holding of this conference is closely related to the victory or defeat of the upcoming Far Eastern Games. The mission is so important that each player should be more vigilant, show their skills, and the satisfactory result can be predicted.

Oath Ceremony 119

Each unit holds its unit flag, leads the captains of each team, advances to the track, faces the rostrum, and reads the oath aloud. All athletes read aloud following the voice. At this time, the general captain will hold the team flag half-tilted and salute. The oath reads: "We hereby participate in the competition in an amateur capacity, in accordance with the late Premier's exhortation to promote sports, and all the rules and regulations of this Games, in order to achieve the goal of strengthening the country and the people. This oath."

Strengths of Each Team

(1) Football 123

Shanghai is the strongest

Too bad the Hong Kong team is not attending

Of the twelve participating teams, eleven remain because Beiping is not coming. Shanghai is undoubtedly the strongest, and can be sure of winning the championship. Guangdong, Tianjin, and Liaoning are second. It is a pity that the strong national team, Hong Kong, did not register to attend. Otherwise, the final could attract thousands of spectators from Shanghai.

(2) Basketball 124

Shanghai, Kobe, and Tianjin have the best chance

This sport has the most registrations and is the most competitive in this All-China Games. According to the investigation, there are six strong teams. First, Tianjin; second, Beiping; third, Guangdong, all above on the order. Fourth, Shanghai; fifth, Kobe; sixth, Liaoning, all below on the order. Tianjin, Beiping, and Shanghai have the most fighting experience and strength. The championship should come from one of these teams. The military appearance is mighty, the fighting spirit is firm, and it is unknown who will be the final winner.

(3) Volleyball 125

Shanghai and Hong Kong are formidable opponents

Unfortunately, they will meet in the second week

Hong Kong is the strongest. Before departing, the team defeated Guangdong. Shanghai is also very fierce, ambitious, and determined to win the championship. The Fujian team, which is not very noticeable, is also quite frightening. According to the order, Hong Kong and Shanghai will meet in the second week, which is unfortunate, because Shanghai and Hong Kong are the only formidable opponents.

(4) Baseball 126

Shanghai and Hong Kong players have not registered

It is impossible to predict the championship

Shanghai and Hong Kong both have very experienced players, but because the Sports Association has decided to give the Far Eastern representative rights to the Tan Xiangshan team, both sides have not registered and only second-class players are participating in the competition, so it is impossible to predict the championship. Tianjin also has a very good chance.

(5) Tennis 127

Shanghai and Guangdong have the best chance

Jiang Daozhang and He Jia of Hong Kong did not attend because the Hong Kong competition was not over. Otherwise, they could be sure of winning. Although Lin Baohua of Shanghai is still competing in the Philippines and has not returned, there are still several good players who can compete with the Guangdong and Tianjin teams. According to people familiar with the situation, Shanghai and Guangdong have the best chance.

(6) Track and Field 128

Liaoning has many outstanding talents

Shanghai is strong on average

Liaoning has many outstanding talents, and Shanghai is strong on average. The championship will be a contest between these two teams. Beiping and Tianjin may also have strong performances and compete with these two teams.

Shanghai, Tianjin, Guangdong, and Jiangsu are all good in tennis. It is difficult to predict the overall championship.

Page 12

Referees' Meeting 132

Yesterday (31st) at 4:30 PM, the competition section of the All-China Games convened a meeting of all referees. Chairman Jiang Xiangqing first distributed the Games badges, then spoke, stating that the various competitions of the Games would begin tomorrow (1st), and that all referees had heavy responsibilities. He especially invited them here for discussion, and expressed his hope that all referees would be fair and impartial. The discussion then continued, and the following important cases were resolved, as summarized below: (1) The referee affairs of various competitions shall be assigned and decided one day in advance; (2) Referees assigned to each venue must arrive on time; (3) If a team is more than ten minutes late according to the schedule, it will be considered a forfeit, unless there are special circumstances, in which case the referee has the discretion to act accordingly; (4) The time of each competition shall be based on the Games standard clock; (5) After the end of each day's competition, the referees of each venue must go to the competition section to discuss the competition matters for the next day; (6) The tennis competition will begin on the 1st, and all referees must not be absent, late, or leave their posts without reason. The above six cases were resolved after discussion, and other discussions were omitted.

Regulations Committee Meeting 139

Hangzhou Electric Report, 31st – The Regulations Committee held a meeting yesterday and decided to strictly stipulate and publicize the important points of the amateur rules to ensure amateur eligibility: (A) Regarding amateur rules: (1) The earliest period for verifying amateur eligibility of athletes is one year, according to the regulations of previous All-China Games; (2) If any athlete participating in this Games is ineligible, the representative of each team should be responsible for canceling his/her right to compete; (3) If an ineligible athlete has participated in the competition and won an award, the Games has the right to revoke his/her title and recover the award at any time after discovery; (4) If an athlete violates the amateur sports rules, the Games may suspend his/her right to participate in any sports competition in the country for one year after discovery; (B) Regarding competition rules: The rules published in the summary shall prevail: (1) Article 6, Section 7, of the volleyball championship, the section on determining the championship in each week of the preliminary and semi-finals, is changed to: "Each week shall be determined by a best-of-three-game match;" (2) "The section on determining the championship in each week of the semi-finals is changed to: Each week shall be determined by a best-of-three-game match. In each week, if the match is a tie, it shall be extended until the winner is decided;" (3) Article 7, "If the case falls to other, extrapolate," is canceled; (4) Article 8, the entire article is canceled.

Method of Winning Championships 154

Men's Championships: 8 events

Women's Championships: 4 events

Also, Men's and Women's Overall Championships

The Games have twelve championships: Men's Track and Field, Men's Decathlon, Men's Soccer, Men's Baseball, Men's Swimming, Men's Basketball, Men's Volleyball, Men's Tennis, and Women's Track and Field, Women's Basketball, Women's Volleyball, Women's Tennis, plus two Overall Championships for Men and Women. The method for winning championships is recorded below:

(1) Track and Field Championship 155

The top four finishers in each individual event will be recorded. The scoring will be 5-3-2-1, except for the Women's 200m Relay, which will be scored 16-4-2. The unit with the most points wins the championship. If two or more units have the same number of points, the unit with the most first-place finishes in individual events wins the championship. If the number of first-place finishes is also the same, the unit with the most second-place finishes wins the championship, and so on.

(2) Decathlon Championship 156

The top four finishers in each individual event will be recorded. The scoring will be 16-4-2. The unit with the most points wins the championship. If two or more units have the same number of points, the method for determining the championship is the same as in Track and Field.

(3) Swimming Championship 157

The top four finishers in each individual event will be recorded. The scoring will be 5-3-2-1, except for the 200m Medley Relay, which will be scored 16-4-2. The unit with the most points wins the championship. If two or more units have the same number of points, the method for determining the championship is the same as in Track and Field.

(4) Soccer Championship 158

The winner of the knockout tournament, arranged by drawing lots, wins the championship. If two teams are tied at the end of regulation time, a 30-minute extension will be played. If the score is still tied, the Organizing Committee will schedule a make-up game.

(5) Basketball Championship 159

The winner of the knockout tournament, arranged by drawing lots, wins the championship. If the score is tied at the end of the game, the men's game will be extended by five minutes or multiple five-minute periods until a winner is determined, according to the rules. Women's games will not have an overtime period; the team with more field goals wins. If the number of field goals is the same, the team with fewer fouls wins.

(6) Tennis Championship 160

The winner of the knockout tournament, arranged by drawing lots, wins the championship. The Davis Cup rules will be used for two-team matches to determine the winner, i.e., four singles matches and one doubles match. Each singles match will be played by two players who alternate games and cannot be substituted mid-match. Doubles matches can be played by any players. Each match will be decided by best-of-five sets. The team that wins three out of the five matches is the winner. This applies to both men's and women's matches.

(7) Volleyball Championship 161

The winner of the knockout tournament, arranged by drawing lots, wins the championship. The preliminary and quarterfinal rounds will be decided by best-of-three sets. The final quarterfinal and championship matches will be decided by best-of-five sets. This applies to both men's and women's matches.

(8) Baseball Championship 162

The winner of the knockout tournament, arranged by drawing lots, wins the championship. Each game will be nine innings. If the score is tied at the end of the ninth inning, two extra innings will be played. If the score is still tied, the Organizing Committee will schedule a make-up game.

Hong Kong Volleyball Team

(Photographed by Mr. Lin Zemin of the Photographic Society News Department)

(9) Men's and Women's Overall Championships 163

The association will award one overall championship to both the men's and women's divisions. The unit with the most individual championships will be awarded the overall championship of the games. If two or more units have the same number of individual championships, the unit with the most runner-up (i.e. second place) finishes will be awarded the overall championship of the games, and so on.

If it is necessary to determine the runner-up for a ball sport championship due to the overall championship, the respective championship committee may order a match between the team that lost in the quarterfinals and the team that lost in the finals; the winner will be named runner-up. The same principle will be used for third place and below. However, if it is not related to the overall championship, there is no need to hold a separate match; the team that lost in the finals will be named runner-up.

Yesterday's Welcome Reception 164

The National Games held a welcome reception for athletes from all over the country at the West Lake Auditorium at 7 PM last night (the 1st).

Reception and Security 165

More Staff Hired for Reception - With the National Games about to begin, athletes selected from the provinces to participate in Hangzhou have been arriving in droves, totaling nearly two thousand people. The association is well-prepared for the athletes' food and lodging, and is especially attentive to all aspects of reception. In addition to group leader Jiang Jiasheng, deputy group leader Chen Xuebai, and group members Yang Peisun and Yu Deyi, the organizing committee has rehired over fifty additional reception staff members due to the exceptionally enthusiastic arrival of athletes from various locations in recent days, as the existing staff members are unable to handle all the work.

Security arrangements at the venue have been thoroughly planned by the security division. Yesterday at 2 PM, the disciplinary committee, intending to foster camaraderie, specially convened the army, police, and boy scouts maintaining order at the venue to have a brief discussion on the command platform. Yu Jimin, executive member of the disciplinary committee, presided over the meeting, discussing methods of mutual communication and disciplinary action, and introducing the disciplinary committee members to the disciplinary officers.

Mr. Feng Yong's Chat in the Train 166

Today is the opening day of the National Games. The train to Hangzhou was extremely lively. Yesterday, important figures who came to Hangzhou included Wang Zhengting, Chu Minyi, Jiang Menglin, and Zhang Wohua. Our reporter also took a special express train from Shanghai to Hangzhou at 8 AM yesterday morning, arriving at the station at 7 PM. The ticket office was already packed with people, as one could imagine. After entering the train car, there was no room to stand in third class, and second class was also full. I managed to find a seat in first class. Soon after, Feng Yong, the president of Northeastern Feng Yong University, and Mr. Chu Minyi and Hong Shen also arrived. The reporter stepped forward to greet them. The reporter had met Feng once before in Liaoning a few years ago. We chatted in the train with great interest. Feng was wearing a black wool school uniform, looking solemn. There was a slight scar on his forehead, a result of the plane crash near Suzhou. Feng said he flew to that area that day, but due to heavy rain and darkness, he had to land. Although the plane was slightly damaged, he was not injured, which was very fortunate.

Northeastern Prodigy Liu Changchun 167

After breaking the national record with a time of 10.6 seconds in the 100 meters, Northeastern prodigy Liu Changchun startled the nation. The reporter asked Feng about Liu. According to Feng, Liu is from Dalian and has a natural talent for sprinting. He could casually run 10.8 or 10.9 seconds in school. However, it is quite difficult to improve with natural talent alone; he needs to add hard and continuous training to have hope for the future. Mr. Liu is currently unwell and his performance has deteriorated considerably, but because the Games concern the whole country, he must participate to the best of his ability.

Climate and Sports are Related 168

Feng also said that the climate in Liaoning is much colder than in the South, which makes it difficult to practice field events. Therefore, Liaoning's performance has not improved significantly in recent years. This is also related to geography. Fortunately, the authorities strongly promote sports and the facilities are quite adequate, resulting in today's achievements, which are not easy to come by.

The Football Team Should Not Be Underestimated 169

The Feng Yong University football team has a strong reputation in North China. This time, they represent Liaoning in the competition in the South, and their strength should not be underestimated. Feng also paid great attention to this. Yesterday, he frequently displayed the football schedule in the train and told the reporter that the school had recently hired Gu Zhian and Li Guilin, two excellent football players who graduated from Yanjing University, to serve as coaches, hoping to train a strong team in the future. His enthusiasm is evident.

Snippets 170

The Female Athletes Are Colorful - This time, a total of 36 groups participated in the Games, and the female athletes numbered over two hundred. Women from the North, South, East, and West gathered in one place, their appearances and clothing diverse and beautiful. The Liaoning female athletes have upright posture and are taller. The Guangdong female athletes are valiant and lively. The women from the Yangtze River region are graceful and agile. The colors of the clothing are mostly deep in the North, bright in the Central region, and exotic in the South, representing the customs of various regions. The Games venue is colorful and interesting. In the setting sun, West Lake is especially beautiful.

Funny Stories about Meal Problems - The venue has a large dining hall with enough seats for 300 people at the same time. The kitchen employs more than ten stokers, twenty cooks, forty general helpers, and twenty people to pick vegetables and wash rice, totaling over a hundred people. Such a large kitchen could be considered an army. However, the dining hall has no shelter, so it is exposed to wind and rain. The weather has been cold lately, so the food is not hot. The athletes have come from afar, and they are not used to cold food, which has caused some discomfort. A certain female athlete from this city could not eat at mealtime, and tears streamed down her face, which was also quite interesting. A European who came with the Liaoning athletes speaks fluent Chinese. He is said to be a ball sports teacher who lives with the athletes. When eating, he uses chopsticks to pick up rice and vegetables, and his hands are almost useless. He has been eating bread with the northern athletes lately, so he is no longer embarrassed.

Precise Statistics of Bowls and Plates - The statistics of all the furniture in the large dining hall are as follows: 240 tables, 960 benches, 1,920 rice bowls (not counting the spares), 920 vegetable bowls, 960 basins, 60 large rice buckets, 1,920 spoons, and 3,840 chopsticks.

Business is Booming Everywhere - A corner near the entrance of the venue is not surrounded by markets, but more and more athletes and staff are gathering there. Cigarettes and snacks are needed everywhere. For the first few days, there was nothing to buy. Lately, vendors from all over have been rushing to do speculative business. There is also a temporary store near the Games dormitory, with daily sales of 70 to 80 yuan, it is said.

Suspected of Being in a Dance Hall - The arrangement of each venue is quite beautiful, especially the basketball venue. The floor is paved with cedar planks and painted, making it bright and dazzling. Those who do not know might think it is a dance hall. When competing, the soles of the feet feel soft and the steps are light. Before the Games opened, athletes came to visit and could not resist jumping a few steps of the Charleston.

Hanli Presents Zhongling Printing Machines - The Zhongling pneumatic printing machine is a new invention of the Shanghai Hanli Company. The machine has exquisite decoration and is easy to carry. It is reported that Mr. Zhongling, the general manager of the company, has specially made two exquisite printing machines to encourage our country's sports talents. They will be transported to the National Games office soon and presented to the male and female overall champions, one each.

Chairman Chiang Smiles by the Lakeside - The area from the Lakeside Road to the Yue Fei Temple was cordoned off by sentries for three hours the day before yesterday (the 30th), and traffic was cut off. It was rumored that Chiang had come to Hangzhou to visit the National Games and enjoy the lake. In fact, Chiang was not on the lake that day. Yesterday morning (the 31st), Chiang strolled along the lakeside, paying homage to the statue of Chen Yingshi, lingering for a long time. Most of the people in the city did not know. Some female athletes from Guangdong were also enjoying the morning light and gazing at the lakeside. As soon as they saw that it was Chairman Chiang, they stopped and stared at him. After a while, he smiled, and Chiang returned the smile and left.

Our Country's Tennis Stars Lin and Qiu Will Stay in the Philippines Temporarily 171

They Will Go to Japan After a Month of Training

Manila Correspondent: Our country's tennis stars Lin Baohua and Qiu Feihai came to Manila at the invitation of the Carnival to join the All-Philippines tennis competition. Because the two had not cooperated in long-term training in their home country, they unfortunately failed. The 9th Far Eastern Games to be held in Japan are approaching soon. Some enthusiasts in this city, such as Mr. Lin Zhuguang, fear that there are no equivalent strong opponents in the country to practice with them, and the climate in the country is still cold and unsuitable for training, so they have been retained here to practice with the Filipino stars. After a month, they will go to Japan to represent our country in the competition for the championship.

Local News

Establishment of Two Courts Today According to the New Agreement 172

Inauguration of Staff from Both Courts and Branch Prison Today

The Second Branch of the Jiangsu Higher Court and the Shanghai Special District Court will be formally established today. Their organizational laws are based on the "Agreement for the Reorganization of the Provisional Court" recently signed in Beijing by Chinese and foreign representatives. The full text of the agreement has been published in Chinese and foreign newspapers without any changes. Shanghai now has four courts, three of which are directly under the Ministry of Justice. One is the Shanghai Local Court, which handles cases within the Shanghai area but outside the concessions. The other two courts are the Shanghai Special District Court, reorganized and established today to hear lawsuits within the Public Concession, and the Second Branch of the Jiangsu Higher Court, which handles appeals from the Special District Court. In addition, the French Concession Court, which hears cases within the French Concession, still stands alone. It is reported that negotiations for its reorganization have also begun, but it is unknown when it will become a court within China's judicial system. Details obtained yesterday are recorded separately as follows:

Handover by the Two Courts: Xu Weizhen, President of the Provisional Court of the Concession, and Yang Zhaoyun, President of the Shanghai Local Court, recently went to Beijing to meet with Wang Chonghui, President of the Judicial Yuan, to seek instructions. They then came to Shanghai to rush the handover. Yesterday was the last day before the agreement came into effect. All staff members of the two courts arrived at the court early at 9:00 AM to organize the files and records of each department, dividing them into closed and pending cases, totaling more than 40,000 cases. They had not finished by about 6:00 PM. Both parties agreed to implement the handover starting today.

Xu and Yang to Take Office This Morning: Xu Weizhen, newly appointed President of the Second Branch of the Jiangsu Shanghai Higher Court, Yang Zhaoyun, President of the Jiangsu Shanghai Special District Court, Xie Fuzi, Warden of the Second Branch Prison of Jiangsu, and all staff members are scheduled to hold a swearing-in ceremony at 10:00 AM today in the auditorium of the Higher Court Branch on North Zhejiang Road. Ma Shouhua, Director of the Ministry of Judicial Administration, who was sent to supervise the oath, arrived in Shanghai the day before yesterday and visited Presidents Xu and Yang for a long discussion. Wang Zhennan, the newly appointed Chief Prosecutor of the Higher Court Branch, also arrived from Beijing yesterday afternoon and will be able to take office separately this morning.

Ceremony Procedures: The procedures for the swearing-in ceremony this morning have been drafted. Invitations were sent to various agencies and organizations to attend. The chairman will be Director Ma Shouhua. The order is as follows: (1) The oath supervisor takes the chairman's seat; (2) The President of the Higher Court Branch, the Chief Prosecutor of the Higher Court Branch, the President of the Special District Court, the Chief Prosecutor of the Special District Court, and the Warden of the Second Branch Prison take their seats; (3) The entire audience stands at attention; (4) The chairman respectfully reads the Prime Minister's will; (5) Three minutes of silence; (6) The chairman confers the seals of office; (7) Swearing in; (8) Admonition by the oath supervisor; (9) Speech by the representative of the Party branch; (10) Speeches by guests; (11) Responses by the President and Chief Prosecutor; (12) Conclusion of the ceremony, photography, and adjournment.

Appointment of All Judges: All judges of the two courts have been appointed by the Ministry of Judicial Administration. The instructions only arrived in Shanghai the night before last. The organization of the two courts includes one president of the Higher Court, one presiding judge for each of the civil and criminal divisions, one chief prosecutor, four judges, one president of the Special District Court, one chief prosecutor, two alternate prosecutors, three presiding judges for the civil and criminal divisions, six judges, and nine alternate judges. The list is as follows: (A) Xu Weizhen, President of the Second Branch of the Jiangsu Higher Court; Hu Yigu, Presiding Judge of the Civil Division; Han Zuzhi, Ye Zaiqian, Judges; Yang Yi, Alternate Judge; Song Yuan, Presiding Judge of the Criminal Division; Du Fuyao, Ye Zaichou, Judges; Gao Junxiang, Alternate Judge; Wang Zhennan, Chief Prosecutor; Guo Huaipu, Alternate Prosecutor; Zhang Linchun, Chief Clerk; Yang Zhaoyun, President of the Shanghai Special District Court; (B) Ying Shi, Presiding Judge of the Civil Division; Xu Wenrong, Ge Zhitan, Judges; He Qi, Li Mo, Pang Shurong, Cheng Shangfeng, Alternate Judges; Zhou Han, Presiding Judge of Criminal Division One; Wu Tingqi, Feng Shide, Luo Renji, Xiong Fei, Zuo Deshou, Judges; Xu Jiashi, Presiding Judge of Criminal Division Two; Sun Yuan, Zhou Daren, Judges; Luo Chongtai, Shen Shumu, Alternate Judges; Zhou Xianjue, Chief Prosecutor; Guo Wei, Alternate Prosecutor; Shen Chenghe, Chief Clerk; Xie Fuzi, Warden of the Branch Prison.

Separate Locations of the Two Courts: Although the Second Branch of the Jiangsu Higher Court and the Special District Court are still in the same location, their internal organizations must be separate. It is now reported that the Higher Court Branch will be located in the old building, while the Special District Court will be located in the new building for distinction.

Busy Staff: Yesterday was the last day of the existence of the Provisional Court and the Court of Appeal. The transition between the old and new was hectic. The staff of the court, from the president down, were extremely busy. President Xu Weizhen drove to the court after 8:00 AM and entered his office to work. The presiding judges, judges, and clerks each finished handling various civil and criminal cases, checked files, and gathered evidence for handover. Because there was no time, the criminal courts did not open yesterday. The police were notified in advance to temporarily suspend the transfer of various criminal cases. The civil courts only opened one enforcement court in the morning, presided over by Judge Xiong Fei. The work of the office staff was particularly chaotic, especially in the office of Chief Clerk Wheeler, because the Chief Clerk had to hand over his duties, and most of his Chinese and Western staff were assigned to different positions. Like the record room, it was also very complicated due to relocation. The record room was originally located on the third floor of the old building and must now be moved to the upper floor of the fourteenth court building next to the new building.

Appointment of Chinese and Western Police: According to the new agreement, the judicial police of the Special District Court should be recommended by the Municipal Council and submitted to the President for appointment. The list of candidates for these police officers was submitted by the Municipal Council the day before yesterday for the President's approval. However, it has not yet been officially announced. According to sources, the position of Police Chief has been confirmed to be filled by Whiting, a British head constable of Precinct 38. In addition, two Chinese and two Western officers will be appointed as police inspectors. The Chinese side will be filled by Yao Jialin and Tao Wendong. Both Yao and Tao are former staff members of the Yangwu Section of the Public Security Bureau and have continued to serve until now. As for the number of police officers, there are also Chinese and Western personnel. The Chinese police officers are also re-appointed from the original staff, including Deng Jiabing, Zhou Jinrong, Chen Diguang, He Xuebo, Tao Wenrong, Ning Menghua, and others. It is said that all-Chinese police officers will fill the position of constables. It is reported that each Chinese and Western police officer will be issued a set of uniforms, which will be worn starting today.

Wheeler's Farewell Message: Wheeler, the British Chief Clerk of the Provisional Court, will return to the Police Department of the Municipal Council after handing over his current position. Most of his staff will serve in the new court. Since they have worked together for many years, Wheeler gave each of them a letter as a farewell message, generally praising the staff for their loyal service.

Precious Methods for Relief Funds 174

Only by Prohibiting the Export of Cash

The Continental Daily reports that due to the extremely strong bidding market recently, people are bullish, causing the price of gold to exceed 500 taels. However, the main reason for this market situation is not due to the sluggish silver market, but due to the export of gold bars. As the number of gold bars available for trading in the market has decreased, the price of gold will naturally increase. It is reported that no less than 15,000 gold bars have now been agreed to be shipped overseas. Normally, there are only about 10,000 gold bars in Shanghai. If such a huge amount is exported, the resulting situation is unimaginable. The only way to provide relief is to prohibit the export of cash immediately.

Minquan Warship to Raise Flag This Morning 175

To Sail to Ningbo for Sea Trials at 2:00 PM

The newly built Minquan warship of the Ministry of the Navy has achieved excellent results in its sailing speed after several sea trials in February. The internal equipment of the ship has been completed. A flag-raising ceremony is specifically scheduled for 8:00 AM today. Before Captain Zheng Yaoshu returns from Germany, Luo Zhitong, Captain of the Weisheng warship, will act as captain and be sworn in. Chen Xunyong, Commander of the Training Fleet of the Ministry, will supervise the oath. The ship's Party branch will also be established at the same time, and the special Party branch will also send personnel to participate. After the completion of the ceremony, the ship will sail to the Xiangshan waters of Ningbo at 2:00 PM today for long-distance sea trials and will return to Nanjing from Yong around the 4th of this month to be assigned to the Second Fleet and await deployment for defense.

County Property Management Office Submits Opinion on Establishing Grain Storage 176

The Shanghai County Property Management Office submitted a document to the County Government yesterday, stating, "Regarding the submission of a reply, we received an official letter complying with the provincial order to manage grain storage, and a copy was attached. Our office immediately convened a meeting of the accounting staff of our office and the heads of the six districts at our office on February 20 of this year. They all stated that the six districts of the county are adjacent to the commercial port and have convenient transportation, so there is no concern about lack of grain, only about lack of money. Therefore, in the sixth year of Guangxu of the Qing Dynasty, Mo Qianling Xiangzhi was approved by the governor to establish a grain storage project, but there was only property and no grain storage. For more than 50 years, relief was provided during famine years and grain was sold at a fixed price when rice was expensive. There was no inconvenience. It was decided to continue the old system of accumulating money instead of grain and reported to the County Government. The county started managing grain storage in the seventh year of Tongzhi and stored 20,215 stones of grain by the sixth year of Guangxu. The coastal land is humid, and the grain gradually rotted, so it was decided to accumulate money instead of grain. This is due to the terrain and is different from the situation in the inland. However, in the thirteenth year of the Republic of China, He, the former military governor, extracted more than 106,000 yuan of grain funds. Public opinion in the area believed that accumulating grain was not as good as accumulating money, and accumulating money was not as good as accumulating property. Grain is prone to mildew, and money is prone to theft. Only accumulating property is more secure, and the resulting rent and interest can still be used for famine relief. This is also what this county has learned over the years and is different from the situation in the inland. Therefore, we are submitting the drafts of the reports of the warehouse directors in the 29th and 30th years of Guangxu. We respectfully request that the County Magistrate examine them and allow them to be submitted to the Department of Civil Affairs, which would be in the public interest."

First Meeting of the Second Municipal Executive Committee 177

Allocation of Duties to Each Committee Member and Determination of Regular Meeting Dates

Old Staff to Maintain the Status Quo Temporarily Pending Separate Decisions on Retention or Dismissal

The second executive committee of the Shanghai Special Municipality, after being determined by the Central Government, held its first regular meeting yesterday morning at 10:00 AM. Executive committee members Wu Kaixian, Pan Gongzhan, Chen Junyi, Yang Qingyuan, Tao Baichuan, Chen Dezheng, Fan Zhengbo, Wu Bokang, and Tong Xingbai attended. Cai Hongtian and Hou Dachun attended as observers. Chen Dezheng was elected chairman by public vote. The main points of the discussion are summarized below: (1) According to the Central Regulations, in addition to the ex officio members of the Civil Training Committee of this committee, four members should be appointed. It was resolved and passed. (2) Regarding the allocation of duties to each department and committee, it was resolved to hold a vote. As a result, Pan Gongzhan, Wu Bokang, and Fan Zhengbo were elected as standing committee members with eight votes each. Wu Kaixian was elected as the Minister of Organization with eight votes. Chen Dezheng was elected as the Minister of Propaganda with eight votes. Tong Xingbai was elected as the Minister of Training with eight votes. Hou Dachun was elected as a member of the Civil Training Committee with nine votes. Chen Junyi was elected with eight votes. Tao Baichuan was elected with six votes. Yang Qingyuan was elected with five votes. (3) The elected candidates should take over the departments and committees respectively and report the details. It was resolved and passed. (4) It was resolved to set the regular meeting dates for this committee as 10:00 AM every Wednesday and Saturday. It was resolved and passed. (5) The number of staff members in each department and committee should be determined by the person in charge and submitted to the meeting for approval. The existing staff should maintain the status quo temporarily until April 15, when separate decisions will be made regarding retention or dismissal. It was resolved and passed. The meeting adjourned.

Land Bureau Thoroughly Investigates Case of Stealing and Selling State Land 181

Chief of the Map and Land Guardian Detained by the Bureau for Questioning

Commissioner for Stamping Deeds Dismissed and Investigated

Sun Fenglou, the Chief of the Map of the Seventh Village of the Twenty-eighth Bao of the Pusong District, and Zong Dishou, the Land Guardian, last winter colluded with Wang Linzhao, the Commissioner for Stamping Deeds in the district, to shorten the price of the deed and embezzle state taxes when they stole and sold more than eleven mu of civilian land located west of Wangjialou on Hongqiao Road in West Shanghai to the American business Dalei Foreign Firm. Zhu Yan, Director of the Land Bureau, learned of this and believed that Sun Fenglou and others dared to collude with the Commissioner for Stamping Deeds to steal and sell state land, which violated national law. Therefore, he summoned Sun Fenglou and Zong Dishou to the Bureau the day before yesterday and detained them temporarily. He also dismissed Wang Linzhao, the Commissioner for Stamping Deeds, in advance to await investigation. Chen Zhen was appointed to fill the vacancy. The deed was also confiscated and the tax payment was stopped.

Inspection of Chinese Silk Begins Today 184

The Shanghai Commodity Inspection Bureau was ordered to inspect exported Chinese silk. After the request of the silk factory merchants, the deadline was extended to April 1. Now the deadline has arrived, and all Chinese and foreign silk merchants have been notified to comply. It is understood that the silk factory merchants have prepared the procedures for sending silk for inspection, such as newly made silk canvas bags. The foreign merchants welcome the implementation of quantitative inspection of Chinese silk trade, which can be fairly valued. Today (the 1st) is the date for the public measurement and baking inspection to begin. The silk merchants of various foreign firms are preparing to send silk for inspection, including Mitsui with 700 bales, Jardine Matheson with 400 bales, and Qianli Lan Lebi Lianna, etc., totaling more than 1,000 bales. Miao Zhongxiu, the director of the silk inspection office, is supervising the technicians to carry out the baking inspection in order, preparing to complete the inspection within 14 hours and issue a public measurement inspection certificate for reporting to the Jianghai Customs for verification. It is scheduled to be loaded onto the Qihua Company ship on April 4 and released for export.

Case of Japanese Ship Sinking Our Fishing Boat 185

More Than Thirty Organizations Petition for Serious Negotiation

Regarding the incident in which the Japanese fishing vessel "Himejima Maru" collided with and sank our country's fishing boat owned by Zhu Aliang in the waters of Wenzhou during the first month of this year, and then escorted the boat owner and others to Nagasaki, subjecting them to various forms of intimidation, it was not until the boat owners returned to Shanghai and reported to the Fishery Guild the day before yesterday that the outside world learned the truth of the matter. The fact that it was concealed for as long as two months deeply astonished more than thirty organizations of stallholders in this city. Yesterday, they specially submitted a petition to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, requesting a serious negotiation, stating in the petition (details omitted above): It is reported that the Japanese fishing vessel "Himejima Maru" was in our country's territorial waters in the waters of Wenzhou on the night of January 26 this year. The fact that the Japanese trespassed the boundary to fish constitutes an infringement on our national rights and interests, which is not permitted by public law. Moreover, they used a modern fishing boat to chase after our country's sailing boats, issuing warnings that were ignored. Not only did they not change course to avoid collision, but they even increased their speed, intentionally attempting to collide, with the intention of putting our fishermen to death. After the accident, they also kidnapped and detained the boat owners for severe interrogation, resorting to various forms of intimidation and keeping the matter secret, preventing outsiders from knowing. It was not until two days after the incident, when the boat owners were released and returned to China, that our nationals were able to learn about it. The Japanese are known for their brutality, ferocity, and disregard for public reason, which has aroused the common indignation of our people. Yet, they still do not repent, but instead resort to even more vicious means and cruel actions, sinking our country's fishing boats and disregarding the lives of Chinese people in our country's territorial waters. If this is tolerated, what is not? If a serious negotiation is not initiated, what dire consequences can we imagine? Therefore, we specially submit this petition to your esteemed ministry for review and approval, earnestly requesting you to promptly lodge a formal and serious negotiation with the Japanese side, demanding compensation for all losses, in order to uphold the law and appease public anger.

The Shanghai Special City Student Union yesterday issued a telegram protesting Japan's exclusion of overseas Chinese, which read: To all newspaper offices and compatriots throughout the country: Japanese imperialists have intensified their aggression against our country and oppression of our people, resorting to any means necessary. Recently, they sent troops to Shandong, hindering the progress of the revolution, creating the national humiliation of May 3rd. Recently, Japanese imperialists have been obstructing and then expelling our compatriots from traveling to their country, uniformly prohibiting them from landing and implementing the exclusion of overseas Chinese. This is a severe violation of the international principle of equality. Their exclusion of our overseas Chinese is no less than an insult to all our compatriots, and their hostility towards our overseas Chinese is no less than the destruction of our entire nation. Anyone with blood in their veins cannot help but be outraged. If our people cannot unite to oppose this, not only will Japanese imperialists become even more unscrupulous, but other imperialists will also follow suit.
