Abolition of Local Security Chiefs in County Areas Takes Effect Today 187

The various local security chiefs (地保) in the areas under the jurisdiction of Shanghai County have already been explicitly ordered to be abolished uniformly on April 1st. The details have been repeatedly reported in previous newspapers. Now, it is found that since the division of Shanghai into city and county, the six districts under the jurisdiction of the county (originally eight townships, with only the three *bao* of the 16th, 18th, and 21st, and a part of the South 24th *bao* remaining, totaling more than 70 *tu*) are all impoverished areas. The local security chiefs of each *tu* are all assigned from those with more farmland (each *tu* having four, five, or six *kun*, which are plots of land), and they are rotated annually. However, when the time comes, there is often mutual evasion, because once appointed, they must make up for the shortfall, and being assigned as a local security chief is seen as an undesirable burden. Therefore, there are no problems with the abolition order this time. However, it is heard that the local security chiefs are requesting the return of the grain tax paid over the years for abandoned graves and households without heirs. Currently, the district offices have ordered the local security chiefs of each *tu* to transfer all procedures to the district, and then the district chief will direct the township public offices to receive them. Yesterday, the county government had already submitted the compliance report to the Civil Affairs Department for record.

Mr. Black Left Shanghai Yesterday Morning 188

Flying to Seoul, Korea

*Wenhui Bao* reports that Mr. Black, the owner of the *Baltimore Sun* in the United States, departed at 9:00 this morning (March 31st) on a Maryland Free State aircraft from the White Rainbow Bridge Airfield, flying to Seoul, Korea. Many Chinese and American people saw him off. Mr. Black's trip is accompanied by two pilots and one engineer. His old friend, Pei Lan'en, will join him in London. After arriving in Seoul, he plans to continue flying to Tokyo, Japan. Then, he will ship the aircraft to San Francisco by ship and then to Baltimore to donate it to the local museum as a memorial to his journey around the world. Mr. Black and others will then travel through the major cities of Japan before returning home.

Final Test Flight of Japanese Aircraft 189

Returned Home Yesterday

The Sino-Japanese Liaison International Aviation test flighted three times with satisfactory results. The day before yesterday, it flew from Fukuoka to Shanghai for the final time, arriving in Shanghai at 3:00 PM, taking five hours and twenty-six minutes. Yesterday (31st) at 8:00 AM, it departed from Shanghai and flew back to Japan. Because the official document approved by the Ministry of Foreign Affairs only allowed four test flights, it will not return to Shanghai after returning to Japan. Formal flights will only be conducted after the Sino-Japanese New Treaty is revised. As the Japanese side has requested that this navigation right be stated in the Sino-Japanese New Treaty, whether this is feasible still needs to be approved by the National Government.

Ministry of Finance Instructs the Shanghai Machine Industry Association to Issue Special Certificates for Tax-Exempt Goods 190

The Shanghai Machine Industry Association issued a notice to Shanghai National Goods Factories yesterday, stating: According to the Ministry of Finance's Customs Letter No. 17140, "Upon investigation, all machine-made foreign-style goods that have been approved on record and are transported from this trading port through another trading port to the interior for sale have been issued transport documents by the designated customs office to facilitate inspection along the way, so as to avoid double taxation. Those that are sold directly at the designated port, in addition to paying taxes at the export customs office and having the export customs office send a duplicate report to the customs office at the designated port for verification and release, are generally not issued any certificates. Recently, because merchants have been unable to provide evidence of tax payment for machine-made goods transported to the designated port, the tax and excise bureaus of various trading ports have ordered the goods to be taxed again. In order to facilitate commercial transport and avoid double taxation, the Ministry has instructed the Inspector General of Customs to formulate measures. Subsequently, whenever merchants declare machine-made foreign-style goods for sale at the designated port and are ordered by the local tax bureau to pay taxes again, they may apply to the customs office at the designated port for a special certificate of tax payment to provide proof. In addition to instructing the Customs Administration to order the Inspector General of Customs to forward the order to all customs commissioners for compliance, this is hereby ordered to your association to forward to all factories for compliance. Please take note."

Japanese Personnel Negotiating Legal Rights 191

Transferred from Abroad to Come to China

The negotiation of consular jurisdiction, a major issue in the Sino-Japanese New Treaty revision, will officially begin soon. The Japanese Ministry of Foreign Affairs, considering this issue to be important, issued instructions to Shanghai yesterday, appointing full-power negotiators. In addition to appointing existing personnel from the Japanese Embassy to take on different roles, they also telegraphed Shigemitsu Gorō, Secretary of the Japanese Embassy in the United States, to come to China to assist with the negotiation of consular jurisdiction. Secretary Shigemitsu has already departed from the United States and is expected to arrive in Shanghai around the middle of this month. The details of the full-power personnel appointed by the Japanese government to negotiate legal rights are listed below: Minister Plenipotentiary Shigemitsu Mamoru, First Secretary Moriya, Second Secretary Horiuchi Shigemitsu, and Secretary Okazaki Hayashide.

News of Chinese Ships on the Yangtze River 192

Shipping Association Agreement: The China Merchants Steam Navigation Company received a telegram from Li Yunliang, Chief of the Business Department in Hankou, stating that there were many goods and few ships upstream, and that measures should be taken quickly to reserve Yangtze River ships for traffic, so as not to allow foreign ships to seize the great business opportunities. Yesterday afternoon, representatives from various companies were sent to the Shipping Association to convene a meeting of various shipping merchants to discuss maintaining Yangtze River shipping. If the Hankou side needs various Chinese ships to suspend service again, it should be assigned by the various companies so that one or two companies do not suffer the losses alone, and business and transportation can also be taken into account. It was agreed to proceed accordingly.

Large Decrease in Incoming Goods: According to usual practice, the downstream goods from upstream are currently in a state of congestion. However, since yesterday's incoming Yangtze River ships, the cargo arriving in Shanghai has greatly decreased. The reasons are: (1) Due to the strike wave in various ports along the upper Yangtze River, the shipping lines are not open, and goods from Sichuan have been cut off. (2) Due to military relations on the Pinghan Railway, combined transport is hindered, and goods cannot reach Hankou. Therefore, the downstream goods transported by yesterday's incoming Yangtze River ships were only two-thirds of what they were a week ago. In the future, due to the decrease in ships, incoming goods will become increasingly scarce.

Yichang Strike: Yesterday, this port received a telegram from Yichang stating that the dockworkers' union in that port is demanding increased wages due to soaring living costs. As it has not been agreed upon by the various shipping companies, the dockworkers' union has issued a declaration that it will implement a general strike from April 1st. From now on, the loading and unloading of goods on the Hankou-Yichang route will not be able to take place in Yichang. Upstream freight transport is being severely blocked. The strike case in Chongqing has not yet resumed, and now a labor dispute has arisen in Yichang. Goods leaving Shanghai will also be affected by the inability to transport them.

North China Shipping News 193

Lack of Northern Goods: The goods shipped from Shanghai to North China have plummeted in recent days. The grain guild in Tianjin has already stopped importing goods, and Shanghai has no rice, wheat, or flour to ship there. Very few textiles are also being shipped. As for Qingdao, due to the accumulation of goods in various warehouses, customers are not picking them up, so they have also telegraphed Shanghai to stop shipping. As for the goods coming from North China, except for large amounts of Yantai salt being transported to the Yangtze River, there is nothing else being shipped. Commerce in North China is already in a state of near-shutdown.

Yingkou Raises Freight Rates: The various shipping companies in this port have agreed that, starting today, the freight rates for goods shipped from Shanghai to Yingkou will also be increased by 10% of the original amount, according to the methods of Tianjin and other ports. Flour and textiles are excluded; all other goods will increase in price. This has already been notified to the various shipping agents.

Exported Ham Must Undergo Inspection Before and After Slaughter 196

Ham is one of our country's export goods. The trade in sales to US territories can be worth hundreds of thousands of dollars each year. In the past ten years, the United States has used the excuse that slaughterhouses have not been widely established in various parts of our country, and that meat has not been inspected before and after slaughter, to prohibit the import of Chinese ham. Its territory, the Philippines, has also repeatedly proposed the abolition of import. In order to maintain and develop foreign trade, the Shanghai Commodity Inspection Bureau, since the establishment of the Livestock Product Inspection Office last May, has gathered merchants who have always been engaged in ham exports to the Philippines and urged them to quickly establish new-style slaughterhouses. All hams going to the Philippines must be made from pig legs that have undergone inspection before and after slaughter, in order to prevent Philippine government officials from finding an excuse and to find ways to have the United States also lift the ban. This slaughterhouse has already been purchased by merchants last winter on Pujing Bridge outside the North Gate of Rugao to build an industry, and the construction was completed in March of this year, starting the slaughter of pigs and curing of ham. After the merchants reported to the Shanghai Commodity Inspection Bureau, they selected veterinary specialists to implement inspection procedures. Currently, the bureau has ordered technician Wu Deming to go to Rugao to be stationed at the factory to carry out inspections before and after slaughter.

The Shanghai National Goods Factory Association's participation in the National Goods Mobile Exhibition in Hangzhou and other matters have been recorded in the twenty-ninth issue of this newspaper. The deadline is 6:00 PM today (April 1st).

Local News Two

The Shanghai-Wusong Railway Steam-Powered Automobile Held an Inaugural Ceremony Yesterday 199

Officially Opens for Passenger Transport Starting Today

Shanghai Station to Be Moved East to Baoshan Road

The Shanghai-Wusong branch of the Beijing-Shanghai Railway, which has been converted to steam-powered automobiles, has been reported on in detail in this newspaper. Yesterday morning at 11:00 AM, Liu Weichi, Director of the Business Department of the Ministry of Railways and concurrently the Director of the Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railways, specially invited people from all walks of life to hold an inaugural ceremony at the Baotaiwan Fort in Wusong. More than 200 people from all walks of life participated in the grand ceremony. Before 10:00 AM, they gathered at the North Station, where they were received by representatives from the railway bureau and guided onto the automobiles. At 10:00 AM, they departed from Shanghai and arrived directly at the Baotaiwan Fort Station at 10:31 AM. After getting off the train, they were invited to the seaside hotel for the opening ceremony. First, Director Liu reported on the importance of Shanghai-Wusong transportation and the process of the railway bureau converting to new-style steam-powered automobiles. Then, guests such as Li Jun, the representative of the municipal party department, Wang Kechang, the director of the naval reorganization area office, and reporters from various newspapers gave speeches, elaborating on transportation. After the ceremony, refreshments were served, and the guests returned to the Baotaiwan Fort Station to take photos. The guests took the original train back to the North Station at 12:13 PM. Starting today (April 1st), tickets will be officially sold and the line will be open for traffic. All old-style passenger cars will be transferred to the Beijing-Shanghai Railway. This steam-powered car currently has a total of five vehicles, which were ordered from the British firm Jardine Matheson in 1929 and shipped to Shanghai on November 12th of last year. Each vehicle cost £4,140. The car body was manufactured by the Wusong Car Factory of the Railway Bureau. It has a speed of 45 miles per hour and 107 horsepower. It can accommodate 14 first-class passengers and 139 third-class passengers. The car body has a volume of 103 feet and 9 inches. The steam car does not use a locomotive to tow it; the engine is installed at one end of the car. The interior of the car is cleaner than ordinary trains, and the ride is stable and fast. There are no second-class seats. Each car is divided into two sections. After the Shanghai-Wusong branch switched to this new type of automobile, there will be as many as 74 round trips per day. The opening and closing of the gates at the intersection of the railway and Baoshan Road is busier than before, which greatly affects the traffic on Baoshan Road. Therefore, the railway bureau has decided to move the station to the Yifuli address at the east end of Baoshan Road. It is heard that the railway bureau has already negotiated with the landlord of Yifuli on demolition and relocation measures, and construction will begin soon.

Confessions of a Madman 200

Mad and incoherent

Haircut and Manchu clothing are intolerable by Heaven

Too many schools are no good

Reasons for killing as such

A madman named Zhang Jiazhen in the South City, in front of the Qunxue Association gate north of Xiaonanmen on Zhonghua Road, killed two people with a knife and wounded one child. The patrolling police officer shot the madman and subdued him. Commander Jin of the First District's Third Sub-precinct instructed the madman to be taken to the Xin Puyu Hall for treatment. Details were reported in yesterday's newspaper. It is now learned that yesterday morning, Commander Jin Dianyang of the First District's Third Sub-precinct appointed Patrolman Wang Zuoxian to go to the Xin Puyu Hall to record the madman's confession and observe his injuries. When Patrolman Wang arrived at the hall's ward, he asked the madman Zhang Jiazhen, "(Question) What kind of business do you do? (Answer) Small business. (Question) Did you have an argument with anyone yesterday? (Answer) Yes, I had an argument with a woman upstairs in the second landlord's house. (Question) Why did you argue? (Answer) Because I bumped into her body when I walked past, and she argued with me. (Question) Since you argued with the woman upstairs, why did you kill another woman instead? (Answer) This was because Heaven taught me to kill her. (Question) How did Heaven teach you to kill her? (Answer) Because she moved customs and habits, cut her hair and wore Manchu clothing, so Heaven did not allow such a dress and taught me to kill her. (Question) Do you know that you killed her? (Answer) I know that I killed her. (Question) According to you, this woman was killed because she cut her hair and wore Manchu clothing, so Heaven taught you to kill her, but why did you kill the child? (Answer) Because there are too many schools, and they are all no good, so I want to kill students. (Question) Do you know how many children you killed? (Answer) I killed two. (Question) Where did this murder weapon come from? (Answer) One was always there, and one was custom-made from the iron shop on Miezuo Street outside Dadongmen last year. (Question) What did you make this knife for? (Answer) For selling beef. (Question) Have you sold beef before? (Answer) I have sold it last year. (Question) Since you already had one, why did you buy another one? What is the reason? (Answer) One for personal use, one wanted to give to the second landlord's younger brother. (Question) What is the name of the first landlord's younger brother? (Answer) I don't know. (Question) Where do you usually put these two knives? (Answer) In a rattan bag," etc. When Patrolman Wang asked further questions, the answers were incoherent and did not correspond to the questions. He was simply mad and incoherent. Patrolman Wang then inquired with the doctor, who said that the madman's gunshot wound to the left leg (which happened to hit the blade) was not serious because it was blocked by the blade. The gunshot wound to his abdomen entered from the right side and exited from the left side, but because it barely penetrated the flesh, the internal organs were not injured and there was no danger to his life. However, the gunshot wound to the back of his right foot was the most severe, and the foot bone was shattered, becoming a useless foot with no need to be kept. It has been decided to amputate the useless foot tomorrow (i.e., today). Patrolman Wang then went to No. 20 Matianxing Lane, the house where the madman lived, to investigate whether there was any conflict with the madman. The woman Chen Zhangshi upstairs at No. 20 claimed to be from Changzhou and her husband was a coppersmith. Yesterday morning at around 11:00 AM, she was washing vegetables next to the tap. The madman walked past her and deliberately touched her hand. She asked him if he was crazy. Unexpectedly, he glared at her with anger and was about to use force. She was afraid of his fierceness and dared not argue with him. Neighbors dissuaded him, and he went out. At around 1:00 PM in the afternoon, the tragedy occurred. Patrolman Wang then inspected the madman's bed and found two rattan bags. Patrolman Wang also went to the area of Miezuo Street to investigate the iron shop. He found the Zhu Wanshun Iron Shop opened by Zhu Along in the Xiaojiu Hua area at the entrance of Miezuo Street. When asked if he had made a knife last year, he said that in November of last year, the madman did come to order a knife, which cost one yuan. The madman said that it was for cutting noodles. Patrolman Wang then returned to the precinct and presented his findings to Commander Jin for approval. The child Hu Hongliang, who was injured at the Nanyang Hospital, was not in worse condition.

Gunfight with Bandits Resisting Arrest on Changping Road, West Shanghai 201

Four Bandits Robbed a Family in Gujiabang

Indian Patrol Hears News and Catches Robbers

Two Chinese Patrolmen One Killed One Seriously Injured

Bandits Escape in Gunfight

Yesterday at 7:30 PM, while the Gu Xuegen family was having dinner in a flat in Gujiabang, Changping Road, West Shanghai, four bandits suddenly arrived, each carrying a handgun, wearing blue cloth shirts and pants, and speaking with mixed accents. The four members of the Gu family were terrified at the sight of the bandits. One of the bandits pointed a gun at Mrs. Gu's chest and ordered her to hand over silver dollars, otherwise she would be killed on the spot. It turned out that Gu Xuegen had won more than 200 yuan in a hui yesterday at a friend's house, which made the bandits covetous. At this time, Mrs. Gu could not move, while the others stood guard. The other two bandits rummaged through boxes and chests, robbing more than 200 yuan in cash. At this time, a neighbor happened to pass by the door and learned that a robbery had occurred in the Gu family. He immediately ran to report to the Indian patrolman stationed at the corner of Gordon Road and Macheng Road. Upon hearing the news, the patrolman, together with two Chinese patrolmen No. 463 and No. 2138, rushed to intercept. At this time, the four bandits, seeing that the situation was not good, broke out of the door and drew their handguns, shooting at the patrolmen. The patrolmen, seeing the bullets flying, showed no mercy and immediately returned fire. At that time, two Chinese patrolmen happened to be patrolling here and joined the battle. For a time, bullets flew in the air on Changping Road, and the situation was very tense. Fortunately, the area was remote and sparsely populated, so there were no accidental injuries. Unexpectedly, while the bandits were fighting with the patrolmen, a bandit guarding the back door rushed over with a gun, and the bullets did not miss, hitting Chinese patrolman No. 463 in the chest, who immediately fell to the ground, bleeding profusely. At the same time, Chinese patrolman No. 2138 was also shot, suffering unbearable pain, and retreated backward. The remaining three patrolmen, seeing their companions injured, were no longer in the mood to fight. The bandits took the opportunity to flee in all directions. By the time the full shift of detectives from the Gordon Road Police Station arrived, the bandits had disappeared. They immediately took the two injured patrolmen to the Bureau of Public Works Hospital for treatment. On the way, Chinese patrolman No. 463 died due to his serious injuries. After the doctors treated Chinese patrolman No. 2138, he was no longer in danger of death.

Eleven Mauser Pistols

Police Refuse Bribe

Yan Ruling Escapes Danger Amidst Over Eighty Gunshots 212

The Bandit Den is on Route Père Robert

Yan Ruling Endures Great Suffering

Exploring the Bandit's Hideout, Over Eighty Shots Fired

No One Injured, Four Bandits Captured Alive

Yan Ruling, a wealthy businessman from Ningbo and former compradore of the French-owned Eastern Fur Company, resides at No. 173 Changxing Lane, North Shanxi Road. Recently, he purchased a separate residence on Route Lafayette in the French Concession and hired workers to renovate it. On the morning of the 23rd of this month, at around 10 AM, Yan drove his No. 8443 car to inspect the progress. Unexpectedly, a number of kidnappers were mixed among the painters. When Yan entered the room to inquire with the workers, the doors suddenly closed, and the kidnappers pointed guns at Yan Ruling, preventing him from moving. Yan's bodyguards, three or four people, were in the corridor and were unaware of what their master had encountered, and therefore were unable to help. The kidnappers had parked two cars at the door and immediately kidnapped the victim into the car, driving west.

Location of Concealment: After Yan was kidnapped, the French Concession police authorities spared no effort in investigating the case. Over the past seven or eight days, they gathered information and clues. However, they did not know the exact location where the victim was being held. Until 11 AM yesterday, Jin Jiulin, the special investigator of the French Concession Patrol, and Western Detectives Feiji Shou and Shi Langdi learned that Yan Ruling was being held by the bandits in a Western-style house at No. 356 Route Père Robert. They immediately dispatched detectives to surround the area and prepare for action. Around 10:30 PM that night, Investigator Jin, along with about 20 Chinese and Western detectives, fully armed, drove to the above location to make the arrests.

Detective Combat: The Western-style houses on Route Père Robert around No. 356 are connected, forming a straight line. The victim, Yan Ruling, was being held by the bandits on the third floor. After the detectives arrived at their destination, some of them scattered and ambushed to prevent escape, while the others bravely went forward, holding guns in their hands to defend themselves. Sure enough, as they went up the stairs, the bandits were alerted and opened fire downwards, like a string of pearls. Fortunately, the detectives had bulletproof vests to protect themselves. They advanced while firing, charging straight into the victim's room, driving back the bandits guarding the victim, and safely rescuing Yan Ruling. During this operation, the detectives and bandits fired no less than eighty shots, without injuring anyone, which was indeed fortunate.

Four Bandits Arrested: While the detectives were rescuing the victim from the hail of bullets, they arrested four kidnappers. The accents of the bandits were inconsistent, including Cantonese, Ningbo, and Shanghai. They were mostly wearing short clothes. Three of them had pistols in their hands. Because they were resisting the detectives, all the bullets had been fired, and they had no choice but to surrender. A total of three pistols were seized, one of which was a Mauser pistol.

Encounter in the Bandit Den: The victim, Yan Ruling, is 62 years old this year. He is usually quite energetic. Since entering the bandit den, his life has been greatly affected. According to his own account, the treatment by the bandits was very harsh. He was only given a salted egg for each meal. There were three or four guards watching him. One, who looked like a bandit leader, often came to look around. A few days ago, he suddenly said to Yan, "The situation is not good now. There may be some difficulties for you. I hope you don't mind." His words implied that he might tear up the hostage. Fortunately, the French Patrol exerted great effort in the arrest, and he was able to turn danger into safety. When the detectives entered the room, the guard was holding a gun in his hand, firing at the door. Yan was greatly shocked and covered his head with a quilt to protect himself. It was not until the kidnappers were arrested that he felt a little more clear-headed. Recalling the past, he was still fearful.

Payment of Security Deposit Required for Foreign Rice Trading 214

The Shanghai Chinese Grain Merchants Association, in order to ensure the safety of its members in foreign rice futures trading, requires both parties to pay a security deposit for each transaction. Yesterday, the association issued a notice to its members stating: "Recently, rice prices have been expensive, and foreign rice transactions have been frequent. Members bear a heavy burden in trading. In order to ensure the safety of its members, the association has revised the regulations for regular foreign rice trading. For new transactions on April 1, each party must pay a security deposit of 1,000 taels per 100 tons. Alternatively, if buying back, the member can submit the association's security deposit transaction sheet for verification and approval to avoid paying the security deposit again. The security deposit will be paid by the trading members themselves into a reliable money house, and the receipt will be sent to the association for registration. The security deposit will be returned when the original account is settled, with the association and the payer both stamping their seals on the receipt. The association will not accept transactions that have not been registered and had security deposits paid in the event of disputes. Regarding transactions prior to April 1, regardless of profit or loss, the security deposit will only be returned after the goods have been delivered and the procedures have been completed. The above measures were decided by the association's staff meeting and will be strictly implemented from April 1. In addition to issuing a market announcement and publishing in the newspaper, we hereby notify members to take note and strictly comply."

Opening of Longhua Temple 215

Longhua Temple in the southwestern suburbs of the city is a famous ancient temple in Shanghai, containing more than 10,000 volumes of Ming and Qing dynasty scriptures and a bronze Buddha from the Jin dynasty, all of which are historical relics. Next to it is a seven-story pagoda built during the Tang Guan Zong period. The surrounding countryside is full of peach orchards. Every spring, when the peach blossoms are in full bloom, tourists come and go, and the roads are congested. Currently, because troops are stationed in the temple, it is feared that counter-revolutionary elements may infiltrate, so, except for pilgrims, no one is allowed to enter the temple to worship. The merchants and residents of the town are panicked, and temporary operators during the pilgrimage season are even more uneasy. Therefore, they repeatedly asked Battalion Commander Lin Zengding to open the temple to allow people to visit and maintain their livelihoods. In order to take care of business, Battalion Commander Lin agreed to be flexible and organized a temporary patrol team to patrol back and forth. The Sixth District Second Branch of the Municipal Public Security Bureau and the Caoging District Defense Corps also sent many police officers to the site to take care of matters. The Shanghai South Bus opened special buses, which were especially convenient. Yesterday, the number of tourists reached more than 5,000.

He confessed to the truth and was indicted. Liu Zengshi also filed an incidental civil lawsuit, requesting that Shen Kuilin be ordered to return Liu Cuilian, etc. Later, the Criminal Court tried the case and ruled that Shen Kuilin was guilty of repeatedly intending to commit adultery and enticing a woman under the age of twenty. He should be punished in accordance with Articles 75, 257, Paragraph 2, and 64 of the Criminal Law, sentenced to one year of imprisonment, and ordered to return Liu Cuilian to Liu Zengshi for collection. Unexpectedly, Liu Cuilian hired Lawyer Yao Jian to draft a document and petition the District Court to dissolve her adoptive relationship with Liu Achun and Liu Zengshi. The wording stated that she had been repeatedly abused by her adoptive parents, because her adoptive mother had each of their own biological children. She was treated differently. When someone came to propose marriage to the plaintiff, the defendants, Liu Achun and his wife, always demanded a dowry of a thousand gold, similar to a buying and selling marriage, and wanted to place the plaintiff in the position of a concubine. The plaintiff did not get what she wanted, so she was frequently beaten and forced to leave home. She is seeking to dissolve her adoptive relationship and seek autonomy in marriage. The defendants, Liu Achun and Liu Zengshi, also hired Lawyer Lu Qi to submit a defense. The case was opened for trial but remained unresolved. The day before yesterday, Judge Ge Zhitan opened the trial for continued hearing. The plaintiff, Liu Cuilian, did not arrive due to illness, and her agent, Lawyer Yao, appeared in court and requested a postponement of two weeks. The defendant, Lawyer Lu, objected, stating that the plaintiff's age has not reached the period of marriage autonomy. The judge then summoned the defendant, Liu Zengshi, to the court for a brief interrogation, and then summoned Xu Yangshi to the court for testimony. Xu stated that she was 54 years old, from Changzhou, and lived on Dongshatan. Liu Cuilian is my own daughter, nineteen years old this year. When Cuilian was just over a month old, I sent her to Liu Achun's house for adoption because I had many children. The Liu family loves Cuilian very much. She is young and easily deceived. Q. Why is your husband Xu Meisheng not here today? A. He returned to his hometown because of something. Please, Your Honor, do not summon me next time, because I am very busy at home. The judge found that Cuilian's claim and her biological mother's, Xu Yangshi's, claims are not consistent. Therefore, there is no legal representative for the case. The defendant should apply to appoint a special agent. The judge ordered the trial to be continued.

Two Women Hang Themselves in Anger 217

It Can Be Said That Coincidences Occur

Xu Zhu's Wife: Xu Zhu's, the 33-year-old wife of Xu Guiying, a salt worker at No. 30 Yuqing Lane, Xinlu, Qiujiang Road, Zhabei, was suspected by Xu Heshan's mother (Xu Heshan being the second landlord) of stealing a piece of clothing that went missing from their house. The mother cursed at the lady at length, greatly angered the lady. The lady cried in pain on the bed. After Xu Guiying returned home, he listened to what other told him and barged into the room. He held his wife down and vigorously slapped her face. The lady was angered even further. She hanged herself to death in the evening. The 5th District 2nd Precinct were notified and have ordered the bailiff, Shen Xiaohe, to make a report to the District Court. Inspector Wang, alongside others, had arrived on the scene and confirmed the cause. He was instructed to prepare the body for burial and await to be summoned for an investigation.

Song Wang's Wife: Song Wang's, the 28-year-old wife of Song Wanshan, a salt worker at Dongcaopeng, Huasheng Road, Changan Road, Zhabei. Her feelings towards her husband were unusually indifferent. Quarrels had broken out regularly. The day before yesterday, the couple had another verbal argument, followed by physical violence. The lady had been thoroughly beaten by her husband. She lamented her bad fate and that she had encountered the wrong person. She hanged herself in secret in the evening. When she was discovered, it was already beyond help. Yesterday, the 4th District Police Station was informed and had ordered the bailiff, Shen Xiaohe, to make a report to the District Court. Inspector Wang, alongside others, had arrived on the scene and confirmed the cause. She was indeed found hanged. It was instructed to prepare the body for burial and wait for the cause of the quarrel to be determined for further investigation.

Pregnant Woman Injured in Car Collision 218

A local woman, Chen Li's, residing at No. 103 Guangzhao Road, Zhabei, was travelling to Qi's house by rickshaw with her granddaughter, Han (24 years old) yesterday. When the rickshaw was in transit through Gonghe Road, it was suddenly rammed into by a platform cart pulled by Zhu Yuwen, a Haimen native. The rickshaw was overturned. Han, six-months pregnant, was thrown out. The fetus was injured. She laid there unable to move. Police stationed at the scene arrived. The rickshaw puller, Yang Wenhua of Funing, and the platform cart puller, Zhu Yuwen, were apprehended and taken to the 4th District General Office. Han's injuries were declared grave. She was handed to the Judicial Section for questioning.

Automobile Crashes into Wall 219

A Moment's Carelessness... Western Jail for One Month

Zhang Haiding, a chauffeur from the French Municipal Council, drove a 752-number lorry to the side of the Patrol Station on South Shanxi Road on the afternoon of the 24th of last month. Through the driver's carelessness, the wall of the Patrol Station collapsed, crushing Wang Jin Xian, a Jiangbei native to death. Judge Zhu, of the French Concession Public Court arrived to verify. Due to the deceased coming from a poor family, he instructed the Tongren Fuyuantang to arrange for burial. The accused awaits to be summoned by the court for investigation. Yesterday, the Patrol Station transported Zhang to the French Concession Public Court for an inquiry. First, the car section head gave an account of the events. Next, the son of the deceased, Wang Yushan stated that his son had died miserably from the crash and requested for justice. When questioned, Zhang Haiding stated that he was only driving at two or three miles per hour and it was truly through temporary and sudden carelessness that caused the wall to collapse and requested leniency. The Chinese and Western judges sentenced the accused, Zhang Haiding, to imprisonment at the Western Jail for a month. He is allowed to redeem the sentence with a fine.

Relief Requests from Two Counties in Anhui Province 220

Chao County: The Shanghai Foreign Charitable Relief Society received a letter of request for relief from the Chao County People's Food Relief Committee of Anhui, listed below. Privately, our county has experienced months without rain since last spring, extending into autumn. Reservoirs and weirs have dried up, and springs have ceased flowing. All elevated fields have not been planted. Even the small number of polder fields which could be irrigated with effort, after planting were then ravaged by locusts and grasshoppers, resulting in a complete loss of harvest for both elevated and polder fields. The entire county has become a disaster area. On top of the devastation of famine, a massive catastrophe has followed, with wounds and sores visible everywhere, and mournful cries resounding throughout the land. The strong have gone to other places to find food, while the old and weak await death. Selling wives and children is heard of daily, and people are consuming tree leaves and grass roots as if they were delicacies. The severity of the disaster is truly unprecedented in a century. We were fortunate to receive an emergency allocation of 2,000 yuan from the Anhui Provincial Relief Committee, and our association has also raised a small amount of funds. However, there are too many disaster victims to distribute the aid effectively. We have only been able to set up porridge kitchens to provide immediate relief. But how can a cup of water extinguish a burning cart of firewood? Consequently, many people have died from hunger and cold in recent months. Now, although the harsh winter has passed, the spring famine has arrived. The disaster victims are crying out for food, barely clinging to life. If we do not continue to raise relief funds, the tragic situation will become even more unbearable.

Langxi: The Shanghai Chinese Jisheng Society recently received a report from Wang Jingzhou and Wu Huinan, representatives of Langxi County in southern Anhui province. They stated that the county suffered from banditry, warfare, wind, drought, and insect plagues in previous years, resulting in a complete loss of crops. Last winter and this spring, continuous rain and snow have caused the freezing death of vegetables and wheat, making the spring harvest hopeless. Two hundred thousand lives are barely clinging to existence and desperately hope for rescue. They also brought a letter from the county magistrate. The society inquired about the situation in detail and found it to be extremely dire.

Inspection Report of the Bank of China 224

The 25th Report

The 25th inspection report of the Shanghai Bank of China Issuance Reserve Inspection Committee stated that the committee members, along with the entrusted accountants, in accordance with the committee's regulations, inspected the issuance of the Shanghai Bank of China's head office and the reserve vault for exchange coupons used by its branches. The 25th inspection was conducted at the bank on March 30th of the 19th year of the Republic of China, with the participation of the Director of the Currency Department of the Ministry of Finance. The results of the inspection are listed below. The total amount of exchange coupons issued was 110,465,634.65 yuan, of which 55,481,905.35 yuan were issued by the head office, and 21,871,905.30 yuan were used by the branches. The amount used by various banks and firms was 33,111,824 yuan. Except for the portion used by various banks and firms, which will be inspected separately according to the original method, the inspection of the portion used by the head office and its branches is as follows: The amount of exchange coupons issued by the head office and used by its branches is 77,353,810.65 yuan. The amount of reserve funds for exchange coupons held by the head office and its branches is 77,353,810.65 yuan, including 46,939,893.52 yuan in cash reserves and 30,413,917.13 yuan in security reserves. The above two items, with the cash reserve accounting for 60% and the security reserve accounting for 40%, were all found to be correct without error. In accordance with Article 5 of the regulations, this is a formal report. March 30th, 19th year of the Republic of China. Xu Kan, Director of the Currency Department of the Ministry of Finance; Qin Runqing and Wang Yansong, Representatives of the Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce; Sun Jingxi and Wu Weiru, Representatives of the Shanghai Banking Association; Wang Boju and Hu Xisheng, Representatives of the Shanghai Money Trade Association; Liu Hongyuan and He Jinyun, Representatives of the Coupon-issuing Banks and Firms; Ye Zhuotang, Zhou Zhongliang, Li Zhiyun, and Xu Jiyu, Representatives of the Directors and Supervisors of the Bank of China; Accountant Wang Zikang.

Jiangsu Rice Federation Meeting of Directors and Supervisors 227

The Jiangsu Ninghu City and County Rice Industry Association Federation held its sixth joint meeting of directors and supervisors at Cuixiutang the day before yesterday afternoon. Fifteen people, including Zhu Zixiang, attended. Zhu Zixiang was elected as chairman and the meeting commenced. The chairman reported on the developments of the past month. Regarding the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce's letter concerning the Shanghai All Circles Construction Sun Yat-sen Statue Preparatory Committee requesting various industry groups to raise funds, it was resolved to acknowledge and pay the Class B expenses. Regarding the Social Affairs Bureau's letter investigating the harvest situation of various rice-producing areas last year and the recent rice storage situation, it was resolved to print the investigation form immediately, distribute it to the members present for completion, and send letters to the chambers of commerce of each county that has not yet joined the association to forward it to the rice industry association of that county for completion and submission to the association. After compilation, it will be reported back to the Social Affairs Bureau. Zhao Zixin proposed that due to the high rice prices, the provincial government and the Department of Civil Affairs should be requested to order each county to convene gentry to raise funds to purchase rice and use the accumulated grain funds to set up bureaus to stabilize rice prices and maintain the people's food supply. It was resolved to immediately request the provincial government and the Department of Civil Affairs to order its implementation. The chairman made a temporary proposal that for each session of the association, if any committee member has an accident and cannot attend, they should notify in writing or send a representative to attend, and should not be absent without reason. It was resolved that the next meeting should inform each committee member to take note.

Weather Report 230

The Xujiahui Observatory's weather forecast at 4:30 PM yesterday stated that a low pressure system forming south of the Ryukyu Islands will move northeast, causing bad weather in southern Japan. Here, the sky will be overcast or cloudy. The coastal areas of the whole country will have gentle or strong northerly winds. Also, in the 24 hours before 13:00 yesterday afternoon, the highest temperature in the local area was 64.4 degrees and the lowest was 45.3 degrees, while on the same day last year, the highest was 65.3 degrees and the lowest was 37.9 degrees.

Free Talk

A Laughing Matter 231

— Sea Guest

A: Is it dangerous?

B: How can it not be? Look at my old uncle, who is sixty years old and widowed for a long time. Last year, he dyed his beard and hair black, pretending to be young. And then, a widow insisted on marrying him, even dragging along three oil bottles (children).

A: Old friend, I beg you to lend me a hand.

B: Oh dear, I only have two arms in total. If I lend you one arm, wouldn't I become a one-armed general?

A: I can't sleep at night lately.

B: Are you suffering from insomnia? Go and see a doctor for a diagnosis.

A: No, it's because I've been newly appointed as the chief editor of a major newspaper and work all night, so I can't sleep at night.

Wife: When a woman marries someone, she always hopes to receive sympathy.

Husband: Then, in the years you've been married to me, have you received any sympathy?

Wife: I've received the sympathy of the neighbors on the left and right and many relatives and friends.

A: I came home late last night. My wife woke up from her sleep and asked what time it was. I lied and said it was eleven o'clock. Unexpectedly, as fate would have it, the golden rooster chiming clock on our wall crowed three times.

B: What did you do then?

A: I had to imitate the rooster's crow, continuing with eight more crows.

The Interesting History of Gold Teeth 232

— Lv Bing

Some say that the trend of gold teeth has become popular recently and its origins are not very distant. In fact, after research, it was found that German goldsmiths were already able to perform this technique three hundred years ago. The Monigan Medical Weekly also published an interesting anecdote about the first discovery of gold teeth based on historical records, which is quite entertaining and can be used as a conversation starter after dinner.

In the year 1593 AD, a German farmer had a son named Muller, who was only eight years old, and one of his teeth shone like gold. At the time, those who saw it were amazed. As the news spread, it actually attracted the attention of the medical community. Therefore, Dr. Hostede, a professor of pharmacy at Hanmusi Dan University, specially examined the child's tooth. As a result, it was determined to be a natural gold tooth, and he published his opinion in Latin, which was later translated into German, causing a stir in society and regarding it as a new discovery. According to the superstitious ideas of most Germans, it was even said that the gold tooth was a sign from God, proving that God was still among the German people. Muller was not satisfied and took the opportunity to present himself to the public, exposing his brilliant tooth for people to see, in order to gain great benefits. Unexpectedly, after a while, white spots began to appear in the middle of the gold tooth, causing many to doubt. After further examination, it was discovered that the natural gold tooth was actually artificially plated. With the truth revealed, Muller was arrested and eventually convicted by the government for deceiving the public and extorting money.

Interesting Records of Jiaotong University's 34th Anniversary (Part 1) 233

— Cheng Zhizheng

The renowned Jiaotong University, established in the 22nd year of the Guangxu reign of the late Qing Dynasty by Sheng Xuanhuai, has now existed for thirty-four years. Although its name has been changed and its departments have been slightly altered, its consistent spirit of advancement has not been diminished in the slightest. Since Sun Zhesheng took over as the head of the school, the interior has been greatly renovated, and it has become more prosperous and energetic. The other day (the 28th) was the school's 34th anniversary. Coinciding with the completion of the new dormitory "Zhixin West Studio," two major events were held at the same time, and the men's and women's dormitories were opened for public viewing. There are many noteworthy things that happened during this time. I will record what I remember and tell the readers.

Splendid and Beautiful: Before the event, the school authorities specially formed a preparatory committee to carry out all the preparations in order to be serious. All the arrangements were very impressive. For example, at the entrance, in addition to the party and national flags, there were also cypress branches and fresh flowers tied into colorful patterns. There was also a long couplet hanging that said "Tracing the reputation spread all over the world, grandly talented thousands of generations, is the highest school in the southeast, counting the years thirty-four weeks" which was also made with art. In addition, the clock tower was decorated with electric lights and the flagpole was covered with bright lights, all of which were ingenious and very interesting, exhausting the ability to be gorgeous.

An Anecdote of Zhu Zhixin: At eleven o'clock, the Zhixin West Studio completion ceremony was held. Bao Yangxingfu and many Westerners arrived. First, Li Zhaohuan gave a speech, stating the greatness of the school's future plans. This is just the beginning. Then, Liang Hancao, a counselor representing the Ministry of Railways, was invited to talk about the deeds of Mr. Zhu Zhixin (Zhixin West Studio is to commemorate Mr. Zhu). Liang said that Martyr Zhu was extremely intelligent. His mathematics all came from ancient Chinese books. He could immediately obtain the multiplication of three or four digits. When he was in Japan, he studied politics and economics, but his mathematics was more precise than those who specialized in this field. Whenever he encountered difficult problems, he would ask Martyr Zhu to answer them. And he could know the meaning of secret code telegrams without checking. His talent was beyond the reach of ordinary people. However, when the martyr was in Japan, he kept a braid and refused to cut it. Even though Hu Zhantang urged him again and again, he would refuse sternly. He would rather die than obey. Some people who knew the reason said it was his aunt's parting instruction. However, at the beginning of the revolution, many party members could not operate openly because they had no braids. He was the only one who could do it. From this, we can know the depth of his intentions. After the speech, Li and Liang unveiled the name, and the four characters of Zhixin West Studio written by Hu Hanmin appeared before our eyes.

The Flower Garden in Front of the Studio: There is a flower garden recently built on the vacant land in front of the studio. A lotus pond is built in the center, and the surroundings are all grassland. The green grass is spread flat, and the shadows of the flowers are swaying. Sitting by the stream is like being in a French park. It is truly a beautiful place.

Hu Hanmin of Shen Zhi's Account of the March 29th Uprising 234

— Yan Qian

Hu Zhantang, the current speaker of the Legislative Yuan, was actually one of the important figures in the tumultuous March 29th Uprising nineteen years ago. In the uprising's organization, Hu was elected as the head of the secretariat. The morning after the seventy-two martyrs died for their cause, Hu and Zhao went to the appointed location with their team. Knowing that the event had failed, they each returned to Hong Kong and reported the beginning and end of the uprising to the overseas Chinese. The documents reporting the beginning and end of the uprising to the overseas Chinese were drafted by Hu and Huang. His younger brother, Yi Sheng, was also a leader in the uprising's assault and served as a revolutionary comrade in the command of the advancing general at the time.

Nightly Ramblings 235

— Bai Sha's Tear Stains

For ten years, I have been trapped in the factory, consumed by mechanical life. The situation is no different from an ox pushing a millstone, with its eyes covered to prevent it from looking around, and running wildly with all its strength. On quiet nights, thinking calmly, I often laugh dumbly and feel sadly. Especially during the long nights, amidst the rattling of the machinery, supervising those bumpkin commoners, country girls, to work hard until dawn, is the most desolate. This kind of life with night as day is as difficult as an ox and as stealthy as a rat. Alas, the plan for food and clothing must burden people so much. Why should I bear this round head and step on this square foot and seek to be a human being?

In the past, the cotton spinning technique in our country was only practiced by rural women. They worked diligently under the lamp at night, laboring to the extreme. What they gained was nothing more than inches of silk, which was not enough to keep one person warm. After the invention of the spinning machine, people invested millions and employed thousands of workers to operate a factory day and night, without rest in the cold or heat. The yarn and cloth produced in one day is more than enough to keep thousands of people warm. Logically speaking, the people's livelihood should be abundant. How can one know that decline and difficulty are still not as good as the past? Ah, Tagore's words say, "I wish the Chinese people would keep simplicity and return to the truth, and always maintain their poverty. Do not pursue the material civilization of others." Carefully savoring these words, are there not deep meanings?

Among the workers in the cotton mills at sea, women account for seven or eight out of ten. They all come from the fields of Jiangnan and Jiangbei. Most of them are young girls and young women, followed by young girls, and then old women. Why do they abandon their life in the countryside (comfortable and natural) and come to this city to live this cattle-horse life without grieving for their suffering? The money environment drives them to do so.

Among the female workers in the yarn factory, those in the fine yarn section are the most splendid. Occasionally, I see some who are dressed in simple skirts and thorn hairpins, with graceful figures. Because they do night work and have no sleep at night, their peach-like faces are like a layer of yellow wax. Those with plump charm are truly like Wang Xifeng as described by Cao Xueqin, while those who are thin and weak are like Lin Daiyu. Others, such as those with plump faces and rich hair like Pan Xueyan, and those who dance nimbly like Li Minghui, are all described by those who like to compare them and given nicknames. The Orioles and Swallows are truly countless. When colleagues are working until midnight and are tired and sleepy, if they use a pen to compare them, they often learn that the fragrant atmosphere attacks people, and the sleeping demons avoid them by three homes.

Female workers with slightly better looks are mostly in a bad environment and cannot free themselves. Because of work needs in the factory, they often have to be controlled by the machine repairmen, adding oil, etc. When they get outside the factory, there is a group of rogue playboys who intimidate and deceive them. The arrival of a bad environment is enough to shake their hearts and they cannot be autonomous. Therefore, they do not find the practices of Sangjian and Pusang strange. Even in Japan, where the textile industry is most developed, once a woman enters a yarn factory as a female worker, her lifelong happiness is over. Therefore, female yarn factory workers are very despised in the current situation in China and Japan.

Acknowledgments: The newly published "Lament of the Mandarin Ducks" novel by Gu Mingdao of Yixin Bookstore. The content and plot are very compact, with both chivalry and mourning. Gu's novels have long been famous in the literary world, and this book is his masterpiece. I received a copy yesterday, so I would like to express my gratitude here and introduce it.

Red Carpet

Miscellaneous Records of Traveling in America by Zhui Yu Xuan 236

— Lai

The next day, many people from the theater world came to watch. All recognized it as true art and expressed great admiration. Therefore, in the following days, the streets and alleys were full of discussions, with Mei's opera as the sole topic. The name "Mei Lanfang" resonated even more in people's ears. The original plan was to perform for only two weeks, but from the opening day, tickets for both weeks were sold out. It is intended not to change the repertoire during these two weeks. According to foreigners, there is no need to change it for three months. Recently, people have been asking when "Yang Guifei" will be performed, but the troupe members insist on not changing the repertoire for the time being, and the theater owner agrees.

The other day, a letter came from the embassy saying that the President wanted to meet Wan Hua and asked the Minister of Foreign Affairs to speak to our country's ambassador, requesting an introduction. He asked if it would be possible to perform in Washington again. This is currently being negotiated. As for whether to perform in other major cities, this is also being negotiated. Columbia University also invited him to perform, strongly suggesting that they could sell out the venue. This is related to status and will have to be considered for a performance in the future.

The other day, a concert was held to welcome Wan Hua. The participants were all playwrights, singers, and musicians, totaling over 300 people. Wan Hua gave a speech, mainly saying that it is easiest to connect the feelings of the people of two countries through fine arts and art, and it is easy to gain good impressions. (The whole audience applauded loudly.) This time in the United States, he wants to study American art to prepare to return to his motherland and make contributions. Subsequently, the president of the association replied, saying that if Mr. Mei wants to gain some art in the United States to bring back to his country, in fact, as a result, Mr. Mei must leave some art in the United States. The whole audience applauded loudly. In the past few days, there have been several welcome parties, too numerous to describe in detail. Photography studios have also asked people to introduce themselves for photography several times a day.

More than a dozen literary giants in New York have come to visit and talk. For example, Stark Young is one of the great writers and a highly acclaimed critic. He occasionally writes his own scripts. Warmth in the Heart (160) 237

— Bao Tianxiao

Chapter Ten: Red Flames Soar, the Balcony Praises the Filial Daughter; Red Carpet Spread, Meet Famous Actors on the Spot

Zuo Shichen said, "So that's how it is." A Jin said, "No wonder, it's no wonder she acts like that. Eating this bowl of 'broken life' singer's rice, people look at her and think she's quite carefree. But there's no free time at all. A-Nan has wanted to see a play for a long time. That day, when she was talking excitedly, young master Ye said, 'A-Nan, I'll take you to see a play on Saturday. Because it's not good to sleep too late on other days. It doesn't matter if you sleep a little later on Saturday.' When she heard about seeing a play, of course, she couldn't be happier, and she agreed immediately. But her mother only thinks about the business side of things. She thinks that letting go of a singer is losing a dollar, but it makes that child feel no relief at all." Zuo Shichen said, "Just for such a small thing? I'll take her to see a play in a few days." He Jin said, "According to her wishes, it would be best to see a whole night of opera completely. Not to sing even one performance. How is that possible?" Zuo Shichen said, "Okay, I'll think of a way to let her comfortably see to her heart's content. But I can only manage one night. I'll be fully responsible for this one night. If it's more than that, the eldest aunt will start gossiping." Just as they were talking there, Ruiyun came out of the pavilion and said, "What are you talking about?" A Jin said, "Second Young Master said he wants to take you to see a play." Ruiyun pursed her lips and said, "What are you teasing me for? You know I don't have the good fortune to see a play, but you deliberately try to tempt me." A Jin said, "Second Young Master said he's taking you to see a play sincerely and earnestly. Naturally, he'll explain it to the eldest aunt. She'll at least give Second Young Master some face." Ruiyun shook her head and said, "I'm not going. I'm not happy." Zuo Shichen said, "Why aren't you going? I'm inviting you, but you're not willing to honor me with your presence. Young master Ye invited you, and you happily agreed." Ruiyun's face turned red and said, "It's not like that. That kind of play is always unsatisfying. Just when it's getting good, suddenly the performance comes. It's like a messenger of death. That ticket is like a soul-snatching ticket. There are even a series of circles added to the ticket. If you're a little late in leaving the performance, you'll be scolded again when you return. What's the point of that? If young master Ye hadn't invited me, I would have turned him down too. Why do you say things like 'honor me with your presence'?" Zuo Shichen said, "Now there's a new troupe of new plays. They've just returned from Japan. They're not professional actors. They're several students. When they're happy, they get together a dozen people and organize a drama club called Qing Liu She. I know several people inside. They're going to have their premiere in a few days. On the day of the premiere, they'll definitely send me tickets. I thought that on that day, I'd invite you to go and see it together. As for the eldest aunt's side, I'll explain it to her. Even if she's unwilling in her heart, she'll have to give me some face. That's why I asked you if you'd honor me with your presence. But you unexpectedly said you wouldn't go. I ran into a brick wall."

The Discount Amount in March is Only Nine Qian 241

The Deposit Interest is Roughly 2.95%

This year, due to the relationship between expensive gold and cheap silver, the market is flooded with silver funds. The use of funds is uneven due to the sluggish market, and the market atmosphere has been sluggish for a long time. The daily silver discount is either borrowed for free or several fen, and it has never reached one qian. Therefore, the silver discount in March was very low, totaling only nine qian. The pull-off on the 31st accounted for only 2.903% per day, which shows the looseness of the silver base. The silver base is loose, so the price of deposit interest is difficult to save. Fortunately, there is a rule that at least it should not incline to within two liang of the people. Therefore, the deposit interest rate in March is expected to be around 2.95%.

A Prelude to the Implementation of Abandoning Tael and Changing to Yuan 242

Wanxian and Shashi Have Abolished the Nominal Silver Standard

My country's currency has always been based on silver taels. Although silver dollars have been drummed up for decades, the accumulated habits are difficult to eliminate, and they are still conservative. General old merchants use the flat color to seek private interests. The silver dollars are of uneven quality, and private castings are repeatedly seen, especially leaving people with a solid basis for complaints, and also hindering the abolition of taels and changing to yuan. In recent years, there has been less and less silver in the inland, and cash delivery is only in name. As a result, the bad example of calling out the exchange and drawing accounts of nominal silver has led to silver dollars exceeding the legal price, and the exchange rate has surged accordingly. Very few merchants have profited, and the society has suffered greatly. Shashi, Wanxian, and Chongqing are prominent examples. According to the report of the Shanghai Juxingcheng Bank, the banks in the upper reaches of the Yangtze River have tried their best to advocate changing to the foreign yuan standard. Although there were many obstacles, it was not implemented immediately. However, in the past two years, the foreign exchange rate of Shashi Wanxian has become more and more crazy. Many merchants have suffered losses, so they are all shocked and urgently seek reform. In addition to Shashi, which implemented the abolition of tael and yuan last year, Wanxian is now also changing to yuan. The silver taels are all transitioning with 7 qian and 8 fen. After that, there will be no so-called foreign interest, and the exchange rate will gradually stabilize.

Food: The Rice Market in the Lower Reaches of the River is Almost at a Standstill 248

High-grade Japonica rice is being transferred to other ports... Medium-grade Japonica rice is selling well in the Southern Market

Zhabei: The market was extraordinarily quiet yesterday, with the source of supply cut off. However, the Northern Japonica rice of upper, middle, and high grades, which had been stockpiled in the river region, suddenly completely opened up, either going to the Southern Market or returning north. As a result, there were fewer than thirty cargo ships remaining in the Zhabei market, and they were carrying middle and lower-grade goods. The quoted price was uniformly 20 yuan. As for the goods beyond the 20 yuan price point outside the customs, it can be said that not a single grain remained. This desolate scene was no different from the end of the year. The supply of Bo Dao and Yang Du Jian rice was also small. Although the appetites of the various shops were good, they did not dare to purchase rashly due to environmental reasons. Therefore, the entire day's market was very calm, and there were no clear rules for any price increases or decreases. Although Bai Yuan rice had a beautiful color, it is also very rare now, and the market is stagnant.

South Shanghai: The source of supply from the river region is also scarce, with only a portion of the South Road goods and a portion of the Zhabei returned goods. This makes the Japonica rice price here lively. Although it is the same limited price of 20 yuan, the high grade is ultimately determined by the thoughts and vision of the buyer. There is no indication of high grade on the goods themselves. The sales in the main streets of both the North and South markets are quite strong, and neither dares to purchase goods beyond the limited price. Therefore, due to cost reasons, cargo owners are transferring their goods to other ports in succession. As a result, the market situation in Shanghai is very quiet. The Soo Tung-gang machine-milled rice arrived in response to the situation and is at the highest limited price point. However, even though it has reached a lofty price, no further batches have arrived. The sales of Bo Dao and early rice from the Southern Road are brisk and disappear by evening, and the prices are firm. Yang Du Xian rice is also very rare now. Although foreign rice has flooded the market, sales are extremely smooth. Both local and out-of-town merchants are competing to purchase it, and the trend is extraordinarily lively. There is no price increase or decrease, and the buying sentiment is brisk and the market is firm. The overall rice situation for the day is increasingly pessimistic.

The March Wheat Flour Delivery 250

Only 50,000 bags of warehouse receipts were delivered

The total number of wheat flour deliveries for March was still only 50,000 bags, all of which were "Three Star" brand from the Zhonghua Mill. All other mills settled privately beforehand or were withdrawn by brokers, so no bags were delivered. Of the buyers, about half were reportedly bought by a certain large mill, and the other half were bought by local merchants, or rolled over into the next month. In fact, very few brokers were involved. Given the current low inventory of various mills, the opening price for the next month may have to be a bit higher. Since the mills' attitudes are inconsistent, squeezing may be inevitable. The total volume of futures transactions was slightly higher than last month. A list is provided below (in units of thousands of bags):

March 　2,813 　May 　712 　July 　388

April 　1,607 　June 　548 　August 　240

North-South Goods: Glutinous Rice Branches are Scarce and Prices are Rising 251

Glutinous rice branches are a specialty of Guangdong, with a sweet and fragrant taste. In previous years, the market price has always been above 100 taels. Last autumn, due to more local produce, it once dropped to a minimum of over 60 taels. This spring, it rose slightly. Recently, due to low inventory and increasing scarcity, it is rising again. The market price in the top shops is already close to 80 taels, more than 10 taels higher than the low price.

Piece Goods: The Piece Goods Market Trend is Improving 252

Local cotton cloth: The trend has been steadily rising recently, likely due to the sharp rise in American cotton and the rare shortage of spot goods from the mills. The sales of fine cloth and fine twill are indeed uncommon. Yesterday, the price continued to rise by 0.025 yuan. Especially the Yang He fine twill is the most expensive, already at 0.705 yuan. Yesterday, the Guangdong brokers transacted 150 pieces. The demand from Shantou, Ningbo, and inland brokers is also high, resulting in insufficient spot goods for distribution. The situation for Blue Double Fish is slightly slower. The movement of coarse cloth for military uniforms has slightly improved. Yesterday, over 200 pieces of Shuangying, Magou, etc. were purchased at 13 pounds. The local brokers are actively searching for Ewo bleached cloth, and over 50 pieces were transacted at the guild.

East-West Piece Goods: The soaring gold price has affected the market for several days, coupled with two days of holiday, with little improvement. However, yesterday, the market suddenly became active. The opening prices of Eastern goods all rose sharply. The Yang Hong Biao all rose by 0.05 yuan, with 6-pound Guo Ju opening at 3.875 taels and 4-pound opening at 3.175 taels. The Hui Guang Xie rose by 0.05 yuan, with Zijing Shan opening at 4.50 taels and Ke Ai Mei Ren opening at 4.475 taels. The rise in Yuan Yang yarn was even more severe, with Dian Qiu Xiang requiring 8.30 taels and Mogan Shan requiring 8.20 taels. The spot goods for Lintongguan Western Beauty are all sold out. The sales of Western goods, stripes and poplin, were quite smooth in the local market yesterday, but lower body goods were even smoother. Hao Shi's Qi Gong Tu opened at 0.335 yuan and Gongping's Ba Zhen Tu at 0.39 yuan, and both had sales. The price of white stripe hemp yarn was firmer than before, with Zhong He goods at 0.2775 yuan and De Ji goods at 0.285 yuan. However, both Chong Tiao have fallen into the 0.20 yuan range.

Silk and Tea: The Silk Inspection Office Will Implement Inspections Today 253

Each piece will have two samples taken... Each bale will have one strip sample taken. The Shanghai Inspection Bureau will begin inspecting exported silk starting today. Therefore, all manufacturers prepared yesterday to pack the silk to be delivered to foreign firms in custom-made canvas bags, sealed with lead seals, and sent them to the Silk Inspection Office for inspection. The Bureau has predetermined to first perform public weight inspections, taking two samples of silk from each piece, with each sample measuring 450 centimeters. One strip sample will be taken from each bale, and the baking inspection will be completed within 14 hours, providing a public weight certificate to be presented for customs inspection and release. Yesterday, the silk market in Shanghai was firm because the European and American demand has not weakened, the price of Japanese silk remained high, the foreign exchange rate strengthened, and European firms had a strong appetite. The Chinese merchants' attitude was increasingly firm. Yesterday, Xinfu and others brought 60 bales of white factory silk into Shanghai, and Dachang and others brought 30 bales of yellow factory silk into Shanghai. The prices were all firm.

Tea Market News After Revival of Russian Sales 254

Since the Russian firms began purchasing Gong Xi tea in the local tea market last week, there has been no significant improvement in the market. Although the number of Gong Xi tea deals reached is 6,000 to 7,000 chests, the overall purchase price is only 24 to 25 taels, and the Chinese tea merchants are losing no less than 40 taels per dan. Russian firms have not yet expressed interest in Chun Mee green tea and Keemun black tea, and recent telegrams from the British and French markets have stated that inventories are too high and sales are sluggish. Therefore, both Chinese and foreign tea merchants have a lukewarm interest, and all tea warehouses are being cautious about lending money for future new teas.

Metals: 2,000 Bundles of Chimney Iron Sheets Sold 255

Thirteen-gauge and eighteen-gauge chimney iron sheets are currently the best-selling products in the market. In the past two or three days, enamel factories have been buying heavily, and local foundries have also been buying a lot. Therefore, over 2,000 bundles were sold in the city, and the market is getting better because inventories are low and arrivals are few. Thirteen-gauge goods are selling for 9.25 taels per dan, and eighteen-gauge goods are opening at 9.15 taels. The actual transactions are most active for eighteen-gauge goods. According to those familiar with the situation, if there are no more arrivals in two or three weeks, the standard price may have to rise again.

Miscellaneous News: Yesterday, 1,789 bars of American silver arrived, worth 2.4 million Shanghai taels.

Yesterday, 740 pieces of Japanese porcelain arrived, as well as 300 boxes of beer, and 460 boxes of Japanese clocks.

Yesterday, 1,600 pieces of American cotton were imported.

4,900 boxes of raisins came from North America.

10,500 pieces of salted fish came to Shanghai from Seattle.

Yesterday, 3,400 pieces of Japanese cotton yarn and piece goods arrived.

1,950 boxes of matches and 1,500 pieces of bleaching powder were shipped from Japan.

1,050 pieces of roofing paper were shipped from New York to Shanghai.

20 automobiles and 200 pieces of machinery were shipped from America.

Yesterday, 1,000 bags of Japanese sugar were imported.

Shanghai Market

Group News 256

Lincoln University Awards Dr. Zhang Deqin a Doctorate: Shanghai lawyer Zhang Deqin is deeply proficient in law and quick in handling affairs, and has always been praised by people in society. Last autumn, Lincoln University in the United States awarded Dr. Zhang a doctorate in law because his published papers were highly commendable and he had served in both political and legal circles, earning a distinguished reputation. At that time, Dr. Zhang had gone to Hubei for business, so few of his friends in Shanghai knew about it. Dr. Zhang has now returned to Shanghai a few days ago and is still working at his office at 141 Sichuan Road.

Wedding Announcement: Mr. Gu Zurong of Taicang, who graduated from Pingda with a degree in economics and is currently employed by a foreign firm and a school in Shanghai, was engaged to Ms. Hong Xiuzhen at the New World Restaurant last night (the 30th). Ms. Hong graduated from a certain women's university in Beiping and is the daughter of Mr. Hong Xingqiao, a prominent merchant in Harbin. The guests were as numerous as clouds that evening, making it a grand occasion.

Ju Chengchang Solely Distributes Zhongxi Star Brand Floral Water: Ju Chengchang, a foreign and sundry goods store, announced that the Star Brand Floral Water issued by the Zhongxi Pharmacy on 4th Malu has excellent quality and a different method of manufacture. Both its fragrance and color are top-notch. In recent years, it has not only spread throughout the country, but also reached Nanyang, Taiwan, Dihua, and other places, which can be regarded as slightly shining a light for the Chinese business community. This sundry goods store at the intersection of Jixiang Street and Avenue Edward VII has signed a contract with the pharmacy to solely distribute this floral water. All sales in Shanghai will be exclusively managed by Ju Chengchang.

Huilo Extends Its One-Dollar Sale for Two Days: Huilo Company on Nanjing Road and Sichuan Road announced that the company has recently received new goods and urgently wants to clear out old goods. Therefore, it is holding a one-dollar sale, originally scheduled for one week. Now, because many people from all walks of life are crowding every day to buy one-dollar goods, it is extended for two more days. The prices of other newly arrived goods are also extremely restrained. Among the one-dollar goods, the sales of sundries, various floral and yarn socks, handkerchiefs, ties, etc., are the widest. This is because these goods are 40% cheaper than during the non-sale period. It is said that after today and tomorrow, the original prices will have to be restored. Those who want to get cheap and good-quality goods should go and visit.

Therefore, business is very developed. Telephone number is 10931.

Wei Ya Restaurant Branch Builds New Building: The Wei Ya Restaurant Branch on 4th Malu announced that since its establishment, the restaurant has flourished. Although a number of Cantonese restaurants have continued to be established, Wei Ya's customers are still very crowded, and there are regrets of being unable to get a seat. The owner of this restaurant has rented the building opposite and is constructing the latest project, using artful decoration and luxurious furnishings. The halls are spacious, and large banquets can accommodate more than 80 tables, making it the most exquisite restaurant in Shanghai. They have also custom-made a large number of silverware and hired top-notch chefs from Hong Kong and Guangdong to live up to the grand patronage.

All the factory's famous silk woven landscape and colorful brocades will be sold at discounted prices. Recent Business of the Guofeng Photography Studio: The Guofeng Photography Studio at 144 Avenue Joffre announced that since its opening, in less than two months, the business has been quite developed. Many groups and individuals have come to the studio to take photos. The studio's photography technicians, Mr. Wang Shilian and Mr. Li Yiyuan, are both graduates of the Paris Photography School. Mr. Wang specializes in portrait photography and has artistic talent, which is praised by artist Xu Beihong. The studio's novel furnishings are entirely original and conceived by Mr. Wang.
